Toujours deg unebdu-nni, et sous pression n yemma, yeddisidi baba ad aɣ-yawi ɣer lebḥer pour une journée. Aussitôt décidé aussitôt fait. sbeḥ zik neddimari ɣer la plage. Et comme di tmurt-agi ula tagnawt teteddu nneqma, ass kamel ur teḥbis ara lehwa. "D acu tenniḍ lukan ad nruḥ ad d-nẓur imaziɣen-nni, dagi i nejmaɛen?", i tprupuzi yemma i baba. "Géniale ton idée!", i d as-yerra baba. Akka, ḥala ɣef tmaziɣt i ttemsefhamen. Mi newweḍ s axxam unejmuɛ, naf-n nna Crifa tecarji d ittafttaren, temmal i yinebgawen (dont nekni) amek ara ddunt temsal. D nna crifa i timḍebbert n ujemuɛ. tenna-k: "deg temlilit-agi ilaq ad mmttafaqen imaziɣen n tmurt ɣef tira!”. Zzin-d iṭabla inebgawen n nna Crifa. Gar-asen dda Allaoua, dda Meḥmud, dda meksem, dda Youcef, dda remḍan d wiaṭas n yimaziɣen nniḍen. Llan daɣen icawiyen. ula d nutni d imaziɣen. Maɛna, ur fehmeɣ ara mara d-heḍren. et comme aṭas ur ten-nefhim ara, uɣalen hedren akken ttarun tamaziɣt. c’est à dire s taɛrabt. Et moi qui pensait belli imaziɣen akk ttmeslayen taqbaylit!? Et ben non! llan mḥme imaziɣen yettmuzuɣen s tɣumit! Yeffeɣ-d Mhenni Xalifi
Aneɣmis (information) yella kan d ameslay gar yimezdaɣ n Ayt Smaɛel seg waṭas d aseggas tura. Meḥsub iɣermanen-is (citoyens) llan ɣilen belli taɣiwant-a, i yeggugen (ibeɛden) s wazal n 60 n yikilumitren ɣef Bgayet, ur tettɛeṭṭil ara ad tettwiqqen s lgaz n temdint neɣ n lḥiḍ. Maca ddurt yezrin yuɣal-d wawal-a n wacḥal-aya d unsib (officiel). Mi akken rgen yimḍebbren n tɣiwant ed kra n yimezdaɣ n taddart ɣer temnaḍt mu ssawalen « Aswel " bac ad walin annar ed ubrid ansi yezmer ad d-yekk ugazuduk. « Nelḥem ɣer umḍiq anda nga yiwet n tezrawt ɣef wansi ara d-iɛeddi uteyyu-nni, syin akin, kra n win yettsayalen akal din, nessawel-as bac ad yestenyi turagt n uɛeddi ". Aya yenna-aɣ-t-id unmazul n uselway (vice-président) n tɣiwant n Ayt-Smaɛel mass Sadeq Rebbaɛi, send ad d-yernu ɣef ssmamat i d-yettak usenfar i yimal. « Ar tura aṭas i yestenyan yakan, llan d tidet werɛad, mazal steqsayen, maca yettban-aɣ-d ur d-nettmagar ara ugur seg tama-ya, skud asenfar d ayen ara yekksen taɛkemt i yimezdaɣ merra ". D tidet, ur ilaq ara akk ad d-tmager tɣiwant tiririyin n « uhu " sɣur imezdaɣ, ḥaca ma yella smenyifen aqaɛ ed ubellaɛ akken qqaren, rnan ttun lmeḥna-nni n yennayer n useggas 2012, asmi rewwun leɛtab, aḥeyyer, adaxel, ed uḥebber bac ad afen tabutayt n lgaz. Ad d-nesmekti dakken taɣbalut n lgaz-a ad d-taweḍ Ayt-Smaɛel seg temnaḍt Tala n Yifassen i yettabaɛen tawilayt n Seṭṭif, dɣa syin ad d-tekcem Buyman anda ara tettwasbedd teɣsert-nni (station de détente), seg wansi ara ttwasseččent ihi akk tuddart n Ayt Smaɛel, send mara tesdaffel amḍiq « Aswel ". Mara yekfu umgar n tzemmilin, ad yettwasres ukaram(dossier) n tezrawt iwakken ad yettwajerred usenfar deg tazwara n useggas-a ara d-ikecmen n 2015. Dɣa, rnu kra n wakud ad bdun yiqeddicen, i nessaram ur ttaɣen ara amecwar bac ad kfun. « S lferḥ d agaɛmir ay nlaqa lexber-a, nessaram kan ur yekkat xilla n yiseggasen bac ad yekfu ". I d-yenna yiwen n uɣerman n Ayt-Smaɛel.
Tutlayt akken yebɣu lḥal atteqim d ttutlyat, mači d-aɣbel. Yelha i wemdan akken ad yissin akk tutlayin n-umaḍal. D-acu kan, asmi ara attres deg weḥric n t’sartit tettuɣal dayen nniḍen. Dayen yaɛnan tutlayt taɛrabt deg t’murt nneɣ. Adabu seg wass n timunent ar ass-a yesnulfa-d tasertit n-uɛareb. Tasertit-agi « teḍla " ɣef t’metti nneɣ, ama deg uɣerbaz neɣ deg weḥricen nniḍen. Akken ẓran wid i faqqen i t’sertit-agi n-udabu, iswi-ines d-aɛerreb n weɣref Amaziɣ, acku ur yettmeslay ara tutlayt n-udabu. Tikta n « el umma el ɛarabiya " tewwi abrid-is…Arrac imaziɣen uḍenen deg yiɣarbazen. As-tini-ḍ ttidiren snat n tudartin. Deg wexxam, neɣ deg berra ttmeslayen s teqbaylit, ma deg yiɣerbazen ttbeddilen tutlayt akken ad meslayen s taɛrabt. Akken i ngar tamawt, arrac nneɣ uɣalen garen-d aṭaṣ n yimeslayen s taɛrabt, cennu-n cna s taɛrabt, llan kra zemren ad ak-inin: " d-acu-tt akka tamaziɣt-agi? ". Ayagi yusa-d seg t’sertit n-uɛarreb! Adabu ur yaḥbis ara dagi kan, yewweḍ alarmi id yesnulfa yiwwet n lɛefsa akken ad « yemḍel " aɣref Amaziɣ. As mi yewweḍ ad « izaɛzaɛ " allaɣen n warraw nneɣ s t’sertit-agi n-uɛarreb, yewwet lsas n t’metti taqbaylit s yiwwet n tikli yecban tin n lafɛa. Aɛerreb yewweḍ tura ɣer yimɣaren d temɣarin nni ur nekcim laɛmar nsen ɣer uɣerbaz. D wigi kan id yegran deg t’metti nneɣ ttmeslayen taqbaylit yeṣfan, s tikta n teqbaylit n zik. D wigi id yegaren lemɛun lakked d yisefra n Si Muḥ Umḥand, lakked Ccix Lḥusin, tagi d Tassekla taqbaylit taqburt, tin ur lemden ara warraw nneɣ deg uɣerbaz aɛrab! Lukan mazal Muḥya ad yini: " Ah a ddin uqabac! ". Akka, myal aseggas, iɣerbazen ssawalen-d i yimɣaren akk d temɣarin akken ad lemden tira d-umeslay n taɛrabt. Tagara-agi, ssiwlen-d deg taddart n Tuɣezza, id yezgan deg t’ɣiwant n Cerfa deg lwilyaya n Tubirett, timɣarin akken ad ruḥen-t ad mmarkin-t iman-nsen-t deg uɣerbaz akken ad lemden-t taɛrabt! Akka ihi, timɣarin nni tiḥninin i ḥarzen taqbaylit n lejdud ad ruḥen-t ad lemden-t taɛrabt ɣer tagara llaɛmar nsen-t, akken « ad s’hetrifen-t " s tutlayt n El Mutanabi! Nutenti yennumen isefra n zik nni lakked d timucuha, ad bedlen-t tikta akk d yidles i yiles! N’na zwina attelmed « ellif d-elba ", netta-t yennumen tettgalla s « waḥeq n Sidi el mufaq "? N’na Ǧeǧiga attaru « baba " d « mama " s taɛrabt, netta-t tennum t-cerru azemmur akken at ssisen zzit d yiniɣman? N’na Megduda yennumen icewiqen s taqbaylit attecnu « ṭalaɛa elbadru ɛalayna "? Ṛuḥ a a taqbaylit ṛuḥ… Syphax.Y
Lwilaya n Tizi-Wezzu teṭṭef amḍiq amenzu deg usefti deg waḥric n uyefki. Annect-a yettased s tebγest n yifellaḥen i yefkan laεtab iman-nsen akken ad-refden aḥric-agi, i wesnarni n tdamsa n tmurt. Maca deg seggasen-agi ineggura, ifellaḥen ttmagaren-d ugguren iwmi ur zmiren-ara, sebba n leγla n yisufar n wučči n lmal naγ lεelf, leγla n dwawi, rnu lexṣaṣ id-yettbanen di ttawilat, am trisiti, amman, ibardan d waṭas niḍen. Γas akken gten wugguren, maca ifellaḥen yettrebin lmal xarṣum wid yeseftayen deg uyefki dduklen afus deg ufus, xelqen-d tiddukliwin akken ad-mεawanen ad-affen tifrat s tdukli i wugguren-agi merra. Si tama niḍen, Tafidiralit n yifellaḥen yettrebin lmal tameqrant « Aksum azeggaγ d uyefki ", n lwilaya n Tizi-Wezzu, tesḥasef aṭas γef yiεewiqen d wugguren id-ttmagaren yal ass. Γef aya sutren timliliyin akked yemḍebren taεna temsalt, ad-qqimen wa ad-sqardcen iγeblan s telqay i tifrat-nsen, s wudem yelhan. Tasqamut taγelnawt n tiddukla ifellaḥen izzayriyen, sḥasfen ula d nutni γef iεewiqen-agi id-ttmagaren yal ass ifellaḥen yettrebin lmal n lwilaya n Tizi-Wezzu, imi tugget seg-sen ur-zmiren-ara i taεkkemt, dayen i ideggren kra seg-sen zenzen lmal-nsen. Γer tagara, ifellaḥen yettrebin lmal n lwilaya n Tizi-Wezzu, sutren deg yemḍebren εlayen taεna temsalt, akken ad-ggren iman-nsen i tifrat n wugguren-agi s lεejlan ilfayda usnarni n tdamsa n tmurt Islam Bessaci Mhenni Xalifi
Ahat tura ugar n sa (sebɛa) n yiseggasen segmi tettwajerred deg yisenfaren n tɣiwant. Tamkardit n Ayt Smaɛel atan sebken lecɣal-is s wacḥal d ayyur tura almi qrib tettwattu. Ɣas ma yella, iban dakken, tamkardit-a tettwarǧa aṭas seg tal tama: mačči ala sɣur kra n yilemẓiyen i iḥemmlen taɣuri, wanag, ula seg yisɣuren iɣerbazanen (établissements scolaires) i ara sɛun taɣbalut s wazal-is seg wansi ara d-ssawaḍen idlisen iwatan i yinelmaden. War ma nesha, belli tamkardit ad tili daɣen d aɛwin n Tidukkla Tadelsant Adrar n Fad i yekkaten dima amek ara tessedles ilemẓiyen, ad ten-id-tesker deg tayri n tira akked tɣuri. Mi tettwaserref dayen tedrimt i yellan tettwar-as i tesga, ifares uselway n tɣiwant n Ayt Smaɛel tagnit, mass Ɛebdun Nasir, bac ad yessuter azal n tedrimt tayeḍ deg lwali n Bgayet ass mi d-yerza ɣer tɣiwanin n Yiderginen – Iderginen, Tasexriwt, Ayt Smaɛel – ass n 2 seg yunyu yezrin, swayes ara kemmlen yiqeddicen deg tebnayt-a i yeqqimen akken d tajmamt, skud ala iɣraben d sseqfat i yellan deg-s, umma aql-itt d ilem s tidet. Maca, akken i aɣ-d-tenna teɣbalut-nneɣ, ulac ssmamat i d-yeskanayen dakken ma texḍa taɣiwant n Ayt Smaɛel ad ttwasemmden yiqeddicen n temkarḍit-a. Hocine.M
I tikelt tis snat, aseggas-a, i ttuwtent tselmadtin deg uγerbaz Mimoun n temdint n Tizi Uzzu. Tikelt-a, glan ula s unemhal. Amek teḍra temsalt? ddurt iεeddan, γef wakken i aγ-d-yenna unemhal n uγerbaz-a d akken yusa-d gma-s n yiwen n unelmad γer uγerbaz, yekcem γer tselmad n gma-s, yessawel-as teffeγ-d γur-s, dγa yewwet-itt. Syin yekker wahraḥu gar yiselmaden d yixeddamen. Mi d-iruḥ unemhal ad iwali d acu yeḍran, yemmuger-it yilemẓi-agi s tyitiwin ula d netta. Tekker ddunit ad telḥu. Iselmaden ḥefsen γef uxeddim s uzekka-nni (ass-nni n larebεa) ufan-tt-id dγa d sebba i wakken ad d-rnun γur-s liḥala taberkan ideg yettidir uγerbaz-nsen. ‘’Aγerbaz ixus si yal tama. Tiqit di yal tazeqqa, ammus γer tama n tneγriyin, lexsas n waman…atg. Lḥasun mačči d yiwet’’ i aγ-d-nnan yiselmaden. Win yewwten, ha-t-an akka tura di lḥebs n leεḍil. Llan wid i d-yusan, ssutren deg unemhal ad as-isemmeḥ, yella gar-asen ula d baba-s n yilemẓi-agi. Am wakken i d-usan, di&amp;gamma,; yimḍebbren, yinemhalen n yiγerbazen-nniḍen akked sandika. Tamsalt tebda, γef wakken d-nnan imi taselmadt-a tewwet anelmad-nni syin yugi ad d-yas γer uγerbaz. Islam Bessaci
Aẓru d win yesεan amezruy meqren di tmurt n leqbayel, u dwin iwmi fkan azal imezdaγ-is, imi ixxamen n sser d lḥerma ttwabnan s weẓru, s yiwen n lqaleb, d ayen id-yernan cbaḥa meqren i tudrin leqbayel. Lḥirfa n wid yettruẓun aẓru di temnaḍt n leqbayel, ur telli-ara n wass-a, telḥad di seggasen, maca tura tenqes lxedma-agi s waṭas, sebba n laεtab meqqren id-ttmagaren deg-s itarasen, imi zik ttruẓun aẓru s wefḍis d tuẓẓal, dayagi id allalen yellan, rnu aṭas n yemdanen yettruẓun aẓru wexṛen i lḥirfa-agi sebba n waṭan meqqren id-taṭṭafen deg-s, wagi d aṭṭan n yedmaren (la silicose), d aṭṭan i yesrewten acḥal d amdan. Γas akken tawilat n lxedma d wallalen gten tura, am tmacinin, rnu ttawilat i saxdamen i uḥareb γef tezmert-nsen, maca aṭas i irewlen γef lxedma-agi tamentilt yemdanen ur nesaxdam-ara aẓru di lebni, imi yuεar rnu γlay aṭas di ssuma. Macca, ass-a deqs n yemdanen i yesaramen ad-bnun s weẓru, imi yesεa cbaḥa d sser swayes ijebbed tamuγli. Dayen i yeğğan deqs n yemdanen n lwilayat yemgaraden n tmurt n Lzzayer, am Lzzayer tamanaγt, Blida, Tipaza, Wahran, tteqsaden-d timnaḍin-agi n lwilaya n Tizi-Wezzu ger-asent Wizgan, Ifiγa, Iεeẓẓugen, ttaγen aẓru inejren. Si tama niḍen aṭas n yemdanen i yesḥasfen γef wid yettruẓẓun aẓru, imi xelqen-d ugguren meqqren i twenaḍt, am wesyax d wayen niḍen, dayen iyeğğan imsebriden ttkukrun aṭas i uεeddi xarṣum s ṭumubilat, amedya deg webrid n lwilaya uṭun wis 251 i icuden ger snat n tγiwanin, Wizgan akked Yiεeẓẓugen, anda iẓra γellin-d s waṭas, isyaxen sebba n yemdanen yettruẓun mebla tesriḥ, berra lqanun. Akka wa maεdur wa d lḥeq-is, llan yemdanen id-yessasayen amεic-nsen s truẓi n weẓru, acu kkan yewwi-d lḥal akken ad-ḥadren γef tezmert-nsen xarṣum aṭas n yedmaren. Γer tagara akken yeqqar yenzi « Aḥezzeb yugar leqḍaε ", yewwi-d lḥal γef yemdanen yettruẓun aẓru, akken ad-harben ama γef tezmert-nsen akken id-yewwi lḥal ad-ḥarben γef twenaḍt d wayen id as-d-yezzin.
Assegas amaynut n yimaziɣen ɣef tewwura. Deg umenzu n yennayer ad ibedd yal amaziɣ ɣef timadit-is akken ad yemekti anwi i t-illan, ansi i d-yekka, sani i iteddu, amek i d-teḍra d s teqbaylit-is. Akken ad yefti ugdud, ad iqazem tixidas n zzman ilaq-as ijga ɣef acu ara isenned. Ilaq-as tiliwa ansi ara d yeggem aman yetteksen fad i yiman. Ilaq-as akufi anda ara d yeddem lqut ara yefkken afud i "Nekk” ines yesmirjiḥen gar yir lemwaji: tid ara t-id yesufɣen ɣer rrif ( lisser / lemnaɛ) neɣ tid ara t-yezuɣren ɣer yimmi n nnger. Ayen yettqqawiten iman n umdan, ayen i tekksen fad ɣef ṛṛuḥ, ayen yettcuddun " Nekk” ɣer yiman-is d idles. Agdud melba idles am umdan melba iles id nnan imezwura. Ɣef aya i neɛreḍ ad nsuk tamuɣli ɣef yidles aqbayli seg asmi tewwi timunent tmurt ɣer ass-a n wussan.
Liḥala n yidles aqbayli deg issgasen n 60:
I wakken ad illal kra, ilaq ad yilli kra. Di tagara n isaggasen n ssettin tasekla taqbaylit tbedd ɣef yiwet n tqejirt: "tamedyazt”. Amur ameqran n wayen iccuden ɣer timsal n tidmi id yettnulfun s teqbaylit di lawan-nni yella s udem n isefra akked tezlatin. Wid is yefkan azal i unect-a, ɛarḍen ad leqmen isufar itararen i tmedyazt-agi d Slimane Azem Akked Cherif Kheddam, wama ayen nniḍen yella kan d isefra n tallit id tezzin ɣef isental ur d nettawi kra i tusna n umdan am tayri temeɛlalt, leɣrba, d kra n wugguren iccuden ɣer liḥala n twacculin di tallit-nni am zwaj, berru, iḥeckulen….
Tazwara n isaggasen n 70
Kra –nni id yellan, i-ibeddelen tagnit ɣef tasekla taqbaylit, d tizlit n Idir " baba inuba”. Aya yella-d di ttnaṣfa n isgassen n sebɛin. Timlilit yellan gar umedyaz Ben Mohamed akked uccenay Idir tbedel udem mačči kan i tizlit taqbaylit terna ula i lqaleb n tmedyazt taqbaylit. Ssin inaẓuren-agi segrewlen liḥala n yidles aqbayli s –umata. Seg assen-nni uɣalen imedyazen n teqbaylit ttemɛanaden anwa ara d yawwin ugar n tatrart ɣer tira –ines. Wakali, isental ɣef I t-tezzi tmedyaz-agi beddlen. Lqaleb n tira yembeddel, lhejna n twefɣa nnig uglugel treṣṣa iman-is di tesga n usnulfu s teqbaylit. Ahat Lounis Ait Menguellet d netta i-ineǧren asalu ɣer tanfalit deg tira s isefra-ines mechuren am "igenni-m trekeb-it tewla", " nnuɣeɣ yid-k ay yul-iw",” teseḍlemeḍ-iyi",” acuɣer", "ixef yettrun", "anida teǧǧam mmi” …Yuɣ lḥal widen yecfan I tallit-nni ttmektayen-d timzizlit yellan gar Lounis Ait Menguellet d Idir Ait Meslayen ɣer usnulfu n tezlatin yesduqusen lexwaṭer.
Ɣer leqruba n Mouloud Mammeri
Kra agi id yellan, i-yefkan udem nniḍen I temedyazt taqbaylit ur d yekki ara s -ugacur imi inaẓuren-agi( id yewwin abeḥri amaynut I yidles aqabyli) i merra llan ɣer leqruba n Mouloud Mammeri. Amezruy yura d akken d aragaz-agi is id ijaben aɛiwed n tllalit i yidles-nneɣ yellan ɣef yiri n ttmattent. Tajerrumt akked illugan n tira id yexdem Mouloud Mammeri lldint tiwwura ɣer tira taɣezfent. Aya yewwid tawefɣa n ugalen imenza s teqbaylit s demma n Said Sadi yuran ungal "askuti", Rachid Alich yuran ssin ungalen " asfel”, " fafa”. Si lǧera n ssin imyura-agi yerna-d Amar Mezdad yuran ungla " yiḍ d wass”. S wakka I yenǧer usalu I teskla taqabylit s yal udmawen-is ama d tamedyazt, ama d tullisin, ama d ungalan, ama d amzgun. Ayen akken yecban, lmuḥal ziɣ yuɣal ɣef yimmi n leqlam.
Deg isaggasen n 80
Ɣlin ifergan zdat n tidmi, zdat n tebɣest, zdat n tismin ɣef yidles aqbayli. Di lǧera n Idir nnulfan-d aṭas n iccanayen d trebuyaɛ irefden tizlit taqbaylit ɣer tqacuct am terbaɛt n imaziɣen imula, igudar, ifeguren, ineṣliyen, Agraw, Malika Domrane, Sofiane, Amɣid, Takfarinas… Ccna amḥadi yuffa lebɣi-s deg irebbi n Matoub Lounes, Ait Menguellet, Amar Kobbi yefkan lmun i wawal aqbayli akken ad yeferfer nnig zrubat yellan ammer ad yinni i leǧnas meṛṛa anwi id aqbayli, amek tella timadit taqbaylit. Ɣer lǧiha n temdyazt akked ccna yenulfa-d umezgun s teqbaylit imi i tekelt tamenzut tella-d tasuqilit ɣer teqbaylit n tcequft n Kateb Yacine "Moḥand ddem tabalizt-ik”. D anect-a meṛṛa id yeṣawḍen ɣer usaru amenzu s teqbaylit id yesukkes Bouguermounh seg ungal n Mouloud Mammeri "tawrirt yettwattun”. Deg isaggasen n tmanyin taḥajurt ɣer tḥajur bedden imawlen n yedles am Salem Chaker ɣer usijhed n uɣrab n teqbaylit s unnadi deg tjerrumt-ines, d illugan n tira ines. Di tallit-nni i bdan ttnulfun-d imawalen s teqbaylit. Amezwaru seg-sen d win yexdem Mouloud Mammerie "amawal amaziɣ atrar s taqbaylit d tenfransist”. UIamek ara d nezger tallit-agi n tmanyin melba ma nbered imawalen id yefɣen deg tasɣunt " tafsut " yecqan tusnakt (mathematiques) a beɛdda adlis n Hend Sadi "tusnakt s wurar”. Imawalen yecqan "tafizikt” akked " tasegda” ( l’architecture). Deg yiseggasen-nni diɣen id yella usnulfu n waṭas n tesɣunin s tufra ttefraqen madden s ddew iciwi wa ɣer wa. Ahat gar tesɣunin tin yeṭṭfen lbal deg akken leqay ugbur-ines d tasɣunt "tafsut” deg ttarun imusnawan imeqranen n tmazɣa ɣer idisan n Salem Chakler, Said Sadi, Ferhat Mhenni, Mouloud Mammeri. Tasɣunt-agi tukalal as yettuɛawed usezrireg akken ad ddlun yimeɣriyen fell-as imia d yiwet n tssadart n umezruy n umenuɣ ɣef yidles amaziɣ. Di lǧeṛa wanect-a id tenulfa diɣen tasɣunt tusnant "awal” yettwasnen di ddunit meṛṛa ɣef yella di lmendad Mouloud Mammeri.
Ait Slimane Hamid Hocine. M
Sliɣ-as i usefru di tikli-s aḍu yewwi-yi unageɣ akin i lmut, ttxemmimeɣ asmi ara mmte: Ttxemmimeɣ asmi ara mmteɣRruḥ-iw anda ara iruḥMa am ṭṭir ara ssrifgeɣNeɣ ad kkfun fell-i leǧruḥWissen dinna ma d-imɣureɣNeɣ ad qqleɣ d amecṭuḥNeɣ ass-nni ara d-laleɣAd d-afeɣ iman-iw di dduḥTamedyazt-is tnuda-d ddunit, igarawen, tuffeg s igenwan, tɣezz deg wakal, teskfel-d iɣsan yeddel, tɛedda akin i lmut, di tallit deg-i anda swayaε ur sεint ara iṛeqasen. S ssut n tmedyazt-is yesbur s uẓawan atrar yennul tameẓẓuɣt n waṭas n yimdaden.
Di Micli ilul-d Ɛmiruc AMWANES amedyaz, tamedyazt tlul-d yid-s, tettazzal deg yidammen-is, talqayt n tektiwin-is yessefruri-tent-id deg yimeslayen, yebna-tent d tibḥirin n yisefra izerben s iɣuyad n tmedyazt:Qqimeɣ weḥd-i ttxemmimeɣDeg yiḍ i ṭṭlam di tejmaɛtCcaxeɣ, ssbeɛdeɣ ruḥeɣSin n leqrun akka ɣer sdatAm wakken di tziri zedɣeɣKul tiɣilt tesɛa taddartTtmeyyizeɣ ttwehhimeɣKecmeɣ di ddunit tis snatDi temẓi-s yemmal ɣer tezlit, ɣer cna, imi yessaweḍ yessekles tasfift n tezlatin maca ur tt-id yessufeɣ ara ɣer ssuq, yeǧǧa-tt kan ɣer ɣur-s acku iḥulfa akken s tezlit ur yezmir ara ad d-yessenfali ayen izedɣen ul-is. Yeddem yewwi abrid n tmedyazt s tmenna yerna icebbḥ-itt s ssut-is akked uẓawan, ayen iwumi neqqar s tutlayt n tefrasist «Le slam", «le slam" s teqbaylit, d aɣanib amayut deg waḥric n tẓuri di teqbaylit. «Iḍudan" d izwel n uḍebsi-ines amezwaru d-yessufeɣ deg useggas n 2011. Deg useggas-agi, 2014, yerna yessufeɣ-d aḍebsi amaynut anda i as-yeqqar «Akin i lmut", deg-s yexdem yiwet n tezlit netta d ucennay Zedek Lmulud, yerna tayeḍ akked tarbaɛt n Abranis.Xas ma nekk-i-nni d amdanKifkifeɣ nekk d usennanTesseɣ akken i tess deg wamanYettnerni ur yettḥarrik dinXas nekk tt-beddileɣ amkanUla d nekk d amdanTt-ɛicin deg-i wussanMi nnerneɣ ad nnerninWissen anwa lawan deg-i ilul zmanNeɣ di zman i ilul lawanNeɣ yeɣleḍ win i asen-isemmanUr ẓriɣ d acu-tt akinAmiruc d yiwen n umedyaz ixedmen imeslayen i tugget n yicennayen gar-asen ad nebder, tarbaɛt n Abranis, Belɛid Abranis, Akli. D, Aɛmer Uqasi… d waṭas nniḍen.«Tibḥirin n tafat" d izwel n wammud n yisefra i yettheggi akka tura, deg-s ad d-yesdakel akk isefra n sin n yiḍebsiyen-ines i d-yessufeɣ yakan iseggasen yezrin. Deg-s ad d-yernu kra n sin ar semmus n yisefra imaynuten ur yellin ara di sin n yiḍebsiyen-ines yezrin, deg-s yal asebter n usefru ad t-id iqabel wunuɣ yeddan d usefru-nni.Isenfaren n Amiruc qqwan aṭas, akka tura yettheggi aḍebsi amaynut, aḍebsi wis kraḍ iwumi iruḥ ddac-ddac.
Tansa n Talsa Mhenni Xalifi
Yelli-s n wedrar εlayen Fadhma Aït Idir, d tilemẓit n 23 n yiseggasen di laεmer-is n temnaḍt n Σin el Ḥemmam, d tanelmadt di tsedawit n Lmulud At-mεemmar n Tizi-Wezzu deg seggas wis ssin (mathématiques), n temna
tufrar-d d tucbiḥt n teqbayliyin n useggas-a 2015, deg umzizwar id-tesduri tzeqqa meqqren n leqdicat n wexxam n yedles n Lmulud n At-Mεemmar n Tizi-Wezzu
Taẓrigt tis 10 n miss kabyle useggas 2015, tella-d s lemεawna n tmahla n yedles n lwilaya n Tizi-Wezzu akked uγarbaz n usensu « Jardin Secret " Islam Bessaci
Tafaska-agi tettili-d yal aseggas, ass n 12 n Yennayer, ixef n useggas n yimaziγen.12 n teḥdayin i d-yufraren ger 48 id-yusan deg yal tamnaḍt n tmurt n leqbayel, Bgayet, Tizi-Wezzu. Imḍebbren n Miss Kabylie i fernen ass n Yennayer i wakken ad gen tameɣra ideg ara tettwafren teqcict i ifazen di thuski (ṣṣifa), deg tikil d wadduy. Yella-d daɣen ccerṭ amaynut i d-yeqqaren tiḥdayin yebγan ad-ttekint deg tfaska, ilaq ad isinent ad mmeslayent taqbaylit akken iwata, rnu γef waya ilaq ad-tesεu aswir yelhan deg ulmud (un bon niveau d’études), i wesebγes n tutlayt tamaziγt.. Ad d-nesmekti belli llala-s n tullas n useggas 2014, d Hamel Damia. Deg tfaska n useggas-a, ḍefrent-d deg wemḍid wis sin, tamsiwt Numidya d yiwet n tlemẓit n temnaḍt n Σin El Ḥemmam, ma yella d amḍiq wis krad tḥarit-id temsiwt Tassaεdit n Wizgan i yesεan 18 n yiseggasen di laεmer-is. Tazrigt tis 10 n Lalla-s n tullas useggas 2015 tεedda di tegnatin igarzen aṭas, anda iḥedren deqs n yemdanen d yemḍebren. Syphax.Y
Mxalafen medden ɣef ayen yaɛnan lemɛinṣṛat. Llan kṛa qaṛen-d aken d lemɛinṣṛat timaynutin i yellan xiṛ n teqbuṛin.Wiyaḍ ttaṛan-asen awal belli d lemɛinṣṛat tiqbuṛin axiṛ. D ttidett, iseggasen-agi inegguṛa aṭaṣ n lemɛinṣṛat titṛaṛin i kecmen aṛ wannaṛ n tuẓḍa n uzemmuṛ.Ass-a, d ttimacinin timaynutin i yellan deg lemɛinṣṛat, acku tuẓḍa n uzemmuṛ tṛebḥed aṭaṣ n wakud. Tuṛa, maḥsub ttimacinin i xedmen kulec, amdan yeggaṛed afus-is deg kṛa n tɣawsiwin kan. D ttidett daɣen lemɛinṣṛat-agi titṛaṛin ɛeṣṛen-t akken ilaq azemmuṛ aken ad yeffaɣ aṭaṣ n zzit, ttṣeffint-ett aken ilaq, ittefɣed yeṣfa, d-awṛaɣ am…uṛaɣ.D-acu kan, wid iḥemlen lemɛinṣṛat tiqbuṛin qaṛṛen-d aken ɣas ma yella lemɛinṣṛat-agi titṛaṛin ttakented aṭaṣ n zzit, maca lbenna n zzit nsen-t ulac! Qaṛen-d belli timacinin-agi titṛaṛin sṛuɣuyen-t zzit, tteksen-t-as lbenna lakked d « Les γitamines ", aken neẓṛa belli wigi asmi ad yali weẓɣal xeṛben, ttuɣalen ulac degsen-t lfayda. Ma yella d lemɛinṣṛat n zik, tigi ɛeṣṛen-t azemmuṛ aken kan, mebla ma yeṛɣa deg tmacinin.Ayagi yettaǧa lbenna-s akk d « les γitamines " ččuṛen s daxel. Zzit n lemɛinṣṛat tiqdimin yettɣimi akenni kan, bnin, as tiniḍ d-azmmuṛ i tett wemdan. Maca, tuẓma n-uzemmuṛ txuṣ imi mači s tmacinin i tettwaxdam, s lǧahd n yiɣallen, aken ttẓeyiṛen lquqna ɣef teqfacin ansa id itteffeɣ zzit ubnin ɣeṛ wemdun. Aṛ ass-a mazal llan-t kṛa n lemɛinṣṛat tiqbuṛin deg tama n Ṣummam. Aṭaṣ n yemdanen yettawin aṛ din azemmuṛ nsen aken ateẓden am zik nni. D-acu kan, tigi bdant « negṛen-t ", imi tatṛaṛa lakked d tmacinin timaynutin ksen-t-as aḥṛic meqṛen i lemɛṣṛat tiqbuṛin, yeqqimen d-azamul n tjaddit, neɣ nnig waya, d idles aqbuṛ.
Di taggara n wenber neɣ di tazwara n duǧamber, azemmur ad d-yuɣal d aberkan, d lawan ad d-yebdu welqa ḍ-is. Imezdaɣ n yal taddart ad d-begsen iwakken ad d-jemɛen azemmur send ad d- ɣlin ideflawen neɣ at yečč uẓerẓur. Sbeḥ zik, ad d-ruhen digrawen ar yigran nsen.
Yal yiwen dacu ara-yawi yid-s n ttawilat neɣ allalen ara yeseqdec I welqad, i wefras neɣ iw ɛebbi uzemmur.
Wa ad d-yawi yid-s amextaf, wa ttagelzimt, wa ttamencart, wa d lbac, wa daɛewin, wa d ahwic……..
Im-ara wḍen ɣer yigger, ad ferqen amahil, igad iceṭṛen ad d-allin suffela n tzemmurt, igad meqren neɣ izuranen ad d-leqḍen di lqaɛa. igad yessnen ad fersen, add-gezmen ifurkan n diri widak ur nettaréw-ara neɣ widak u yettaǧ ǧan-ara aseklu ad d-yegmu akken iwata axaṭer ttzagan-d i lhawa, i tafat akked d yitij akken ad d-awḍen ar wul useklu. ɣef lewhi n 12:30, ad d-zzin d agraw ɣef leḥcic ad ččen.yal yiwen dacu id yewwi. wa d berkukes, wa d seksu, wa d ameqful, wa ttaberbuct, wa ttiɣrifin, wa ttazart d zit…
Deq ugama, ayen teččiḍ d aẓidan, yesɛa lbenna. Ḥemmar bussaɛd
Ticki fuken učči, add- uɣalen srid ɣer umahil, ulac asgunfu. Ad kemmlen amahil alama qrib ad d-yader yitij, imir ad d- uɣalen saxxam.win yesɛan aɣyul neɣ aserdun, ad yural dafessas ma d win u nessɛa-ra iɣersiwen, ad d- iɛebbi icekaren uzemmur ɣef tuyat-is neɣ ɣef uzagur-is. Im-ara wḍen s axxam, tidi tettcercur maca ɛeggu yettaffeg, lferḥ yettnerni im-ara walin zzit ittemcerqi am awraɣ di lemɛinṣra.
Mḥend d yiwen uzzayri ikerhen iman-is. Netta akked lmeḥna d tizyiwin, akken id lulen, ur yessin ad iɣer neɣ ad yaru. Asmi yekcem ɣer uɣerbaz yezga weswir-ines ulac, yettɛawad kan i iseggasen, ɛyan deg-s ula d iselmaden-ines dɣa ḍeggrent ɣer uzniq yerwa nemḍar deg yiberdan. Asmi yeɛya deg umeṭar deg yiberdan n taddart iqelleb ùef uxeddim. Maca ala lexdayem yenɛettaben i t-id isaḥḥen. Yendem alarmi dayen kan imi ur as-yefki ara azal i leqraya. Maca ndama tettas-d taneggarut. Mḥend yettidir tudert n uydi. Ixeddem aṭas, yettaɣ ciṭuḥ n yidrimen. Yesɛa 40 n yiseggasen, ad t-waliḍ ad as-tiniḍ 80 n yiseggasen i yesɛa. anyir-is yeččur d tiregwa ad as-tiniḍ d amekraz itent-ikerzen. Allen-is nexrent ɣer sdaxel, lqedd-is yekna, arqiq m umesmar, iɣsan-is ttbanen-d ɣef uglim-ines. Asmi yewweḍ tizi n zwaǧ, yettqellib tinna d wara yezdi lmeḥna-s. anda yewweḍ, ɣer tinna yewweḍ ad d-tefk 3 yesteqsiyen -Ma teɣriḍ? -Ma txeddmeḍ?
-Ma tettaɣeḍ aṭas?
-Ur teɣiriḍ, ur tettaɣeḍ aṭas, yerna t-ḍemɛeḍ ad taɣeḍ yelli. Tenwiḍ ad tidireḍ tayri d waman isemmaḍen, ruḥ ad tt-leɛbeḍ ɣef yiman-ik.
Alarmi yerwa tid-ak yuran i yufa tameṭṭut icuban ɣur-s. ur teɣri, ur tezyin, ad as-tiniḍ teffeɣ-d srid si ǧahennama. Yesɛa-d ṭeẓẓina n yigerdan yid-s.
Mi ifukk lxedma-s, yekreh ad yekcem s axxam acku yal yiwen yettsuɣu: -Aɣ-iyi-d aqrab! -Awi-yi-d ayefki! -Awi-yi-d zzit!
-Xelles aman akked trisiti!
Mḥend yezga yettazal deffir texbizt, anda tella ad tt-yeḍfer, nettat treggel fell-as. Yerwa lemrar fell-as, tectaq-as iḍes. Yal ass yettnekkar send ad yecreq yiṭij, fell-as yedda ḥafi, yeqbel ddel. Yezga yettsuɣ fell-as umɛellem-ines, netta yessussum kan akken ad tt-dum fell-as texbizt-is, acku axeddim ixus, fell-as ur yeǧǧi amkan, yexdm di seḥra i iṭij yesserɣayen, yexdem deg udrar i ugris igezzmen imeẓẓuɣen. Fell-as yexdem acḥal n tɣawsiwin. Yexdem d imaswaten, yessareǧ isebbaḍen, iferreɣ acḥal n tzebbalin, yenɣec acḥal d isekla, iɛebba ayen ẓẓayen, asɣar, lyajur, ssiman…
Tagara teǧǧat tezmert, laɛqel-is yexser, yuɣal i teddu dg ubrid yeshetrif, yettcuddu taxbizt s lxiḍ ɣer wammas-is, yezzuɣur-itt, yekkat-itt yeqqar-as:
-Acḥal-aya ṭafareɣ-kem kemm treggleḍ fell-i, tura tezzi-d nnuba-m d kemm-i ara iyi-d-iḍefren.
Deg talγuγa n Tefriqt n’’Echecs’’ i d-yellan di tmurt n Tunes si 20 armi 28 deg duğember, tamurt n Lezzayer tewwi-d 14 n cciεat, gar-asent 4 n ddheb.
Gar wid i d-yufraren deg talγuγa-agi, ad naf Yaristan Yettouche n temdint n Tizi Ouzou i yewwin amḍiq wis sin n Tefriqt deg uḥric n yimeẓyanen. Mačči d tikkelt tamezwarut i d-yufrar unelmaden-a i yeqqaren deg uγerbaz amenzu ‘’Mimoun Moh Arezki’’ n temdint n Tizi Ouzou imi yewwi, yakan, tlata n tikal talγuγa n Lezzayer deg yiseggasen: 2012/2013/2014. Am waken i yewwi tafaska n Sidi Belabes deg useggas n 2011. Yurar, di&amp;gamma,; talaγuγa n umaḍal deg useggas n 2014.
Afud igerrzen i Yaristan, anadal n uzekka, ladγa imi yesdukkel tiḥerci deg waddal d leqraya. <span style="white-space: pre;"> Hocine.M
Teḍrat-tt yid-sen am uzegḍuf gar lɛecba, llan kan i wakken ad leqben deg widen i ten-yiffen. Iles-nsen yeččur d ssem. Ul –nsen izdeɣ-it dɣel. Ɣef udem-nsen yedbaɛ nḥas. Tala-nni ansi id ttagmen tezga tluɣ. Lefhem-nsen yifi-t fiḥel. Tillin-nsen yifi-tt ulac. Lhem-nsen d tunya deg iqera n wid i –ten ibeɛden. Deg akken lhan-d d wiyaḍ ttun akmaz deg ujeǧiḍ-nsen. Akka i d cetla-nsen. Ḥamlen ad simsen leqlam s tedwet n karuh. Ḥamlen terda s ilefḍen. Akka id sekka-nsen, akka i d-tara seg id uɣan aẓar. Mejir d awezɣi ad ibeddel, meruyet d awezɣi ad yiẓiḍ. Yella deg awal: "abequq ẓdit neɣ qqim muḥal ad ineggi s tamemt”. Iqananen-agi, kecmen ɣer yal amkan, ḥaren imeḍqen ur ǧǧin tirni. Nettaf-iten deg iɣmisen, deg lakulat, deg allalen u miṣweḍ, di leqhawi, deg leswaq, deg lintenet … anda yedda umdan ad yidsen yemlil. Ɣer uqajem akked regmat ulac win ara ten-yezwiren. Lferḥ-nsen mi ara hamjen s yiles deg wid iqedcen di tmusni. Anagaru ḥuzzen s yicer –nsen d Lounis Ait Menguellet s timad-is menbeɛd tameɣra yexdem i lmend n yanayer di tzeqa n " zenith " n Lpari di tmurt n Franṣa assen n 11 janvier yezrin.
Acu is id suksen? Suksen-as-id addud id ibedd akked "Charlie Hebdo ", suksen-as-d imi id isuɣ yenna: nekk d Matoub Lounes, d Tahar Djaout…amzun akken alarmi d ass-asen id ibaggen Lounis Ait Mneguellet ibeddi-ines ɣer tama n wid yeɣlin s terṣasin n tiselbi n widen ijeɛlen " Ṛebbi” d ayla-nsen kan nitni. Yuɣ lḥal Lounis Ait Menguellet urd yeɣli ara akked ugafur anagaru ɣer unnar n umenuɣ ɣef izerfan akked tilleli. Si zzman di yenna:
Win iɣ-d yussan
Yewwid ṛṛebi-s d amɛiwen
Anida iɣ-id ufan
Iɣ-ǧǧan widen iruḥen
Kemlen id yegran
Ala d ṛṛebbi d ayla-nsen.
Acimi.. acimi …. acimi…
Meɛna tiɛazegt yesɛab lehlak-is. Akka id as-tedṛa i "umesjarnan” n teɛrabt "ElChourouk” id yesrekkcen lehḍur-is magal amedyaz yellan d aktay n tmurt n leqbayal Lounis Ait Menguellet. Ɣer imayaten n leqbyael Lounis Ait Menguellet d azamul n-usirem, d abrid ɣer yiseɣ. Qarren s teqbaylit: " leqela n lefhem tetterew-d leɛrur”. Yuɣ lḥal leɛrur si zik id ccer ( imi awal d aciri mačči d asmiri) fell-asen Lounis Ait Menguellet s timad-is:
Ur ttaggad leḥrur
Lbaṭel ur tesnen
Ur qeblen ẓẓur
Mi ara k-id qesden Nettaged leɛrur
Ur nesɛi ifaden
Ma zegden lehḍur Alarami tteklen….
Ayen ɣef i tteklen
Ur as tezmired –ara Taqaɛet ixxamen
Iqjan d iqera
Xemsin mi ara mten
Ad ɛiwden meyya.
Akka di yal zzman, ticki yeqwa useglaf di tejmayɛit ikeffu ṣṣwab. Tenza leḥya am akken qqaren deg tmacahut "la ḥya la ḥamra, leḥbab n ɛmara”. Xuḍi, tɛedda tallit yiwen ur yezmir ad innal acebub seg inaẓuren-nneɣ. Di tallit-nni nezdi wa ɣer wa acku tḥarseɣ-id lmerta. Ass-a mi nemyebḍa am ibawen ɣef lluḥ, wa ijebbed wayeḍ ikerref win id yussan yezmer ad yewwet di Lounis, deg Idir, deg Ferhat, deg Ait Ahmed, deg Mouloud Mammeri ma n nekni neḍḥa-d neggugem nettwali. Tidet yerrez ufrag n lḥerma-nneɣ. Yeftutes ublâd n yiseɣ-nneɣ. Yedegdeg ubruy n lɛaz-nneɣ. Terki teswiɛit alarmi tikkwal d atmaten-nneɣ s timad-nsen iɣ yettawin di leɣlaḍ. Yuffa-d uxṣim tabrujt akken ad iɛeddi ɣer tasga. Wama si zik neqqar: " a baba wwten-nneɣ, yenna-as a mmi ɛeqlen-nneɣ.” Lounis Ait Menguellet icer diɣ ɣef tadyant-agi:
Afcal-ik anda tufan
Mi asen-yehwa neɣ mi stufan
Snen ad jebden lexyuḍ
Wis ma d ul-ik I yelhan
Neɣ imi tesɛiḍ laman
Ik faqen amek I tetteduḍ
Ak id awin di nnican
Rran-k sanda bɣan telḥuḍ
Asmi bbḍan ayen yak bɣan
Ǧǧan-ak allen-ik a ttruḍ.
Yeqqar diɣen Lounis Ait Menguellet:
Acḥal I tecbeḥ lfetna
D waxṣim id yefka lḥal
Talluft akken ibɣu tella
Tettban sseba n cwal
I waxsim ad yenulfun
Ma ak id yekk seg axxam-ik
Ma tesusmeḍ rebḥen yisɣan
Ma tewteḍ a tt-ḥaẓeḍ d iman-ik.
Akka id aɣ teḍra nekni s leqbayel( asmi teqaraɛen tiɛdawin/ azger ur teẓrin/ mi isen yesexrab aẓeṭṭa) yal mi ara newwet tiyita ziɣ deg iman-nneɣ. Meɣrud iɣ-yeblan, werǧin nessin udem-is almi d tinegura agi. Wama lemmer am zik, tili d awezɣi ad yeṣṣiweḍ umesjernan am "el chourouk” ad ihamej s wawal deg Lounis Ait Menguellet. Lemmer am zik d awezɣi a yettwagdel usarag n umyaru Kamal Daoud deg tasdawit n Tizi Wezzu. Lemmer am zik d awezɣi ad yettweɛzel Zedek Mouloud. Qqaren zik leqbayel: "ma ikcem-ak ucengu s-amdiq &amp;nbsp,;d agma-k id yuffa d arfiq! ". Teḥfa tadukli n isaggasen-nni deg nemyaɛqal anwi id nekni. Ussan-nni deg yenna Matoub Lounes mi yettwet s ṛṣas di Michelet: Zik ttaggadeɣ
Gma ad yi-ɣder Assa-gi thadneɣ
S idis-iw yehḍer
Mi yesla reẓeɣ nṭareɣ
Di ttnaṣfa n Jerjer
Yenna-yi ad suɣeɣ
Terwa ak-tt-id jemɛeɣ
Ak-id nneɣ leɛmer”.
Necfa yak ɣef wamek id tezdi tmurt ɣer tama n Lounes Matoub yellan di ccedda. Necfa diɣ amek is rran ṣerf-is leqbayel i Abdalah Kriou asmi id yewwet deg Lounis Ait. Necfa diɣ amek is zmemen immi i umesjrnan Ouazani n "Algérie Actualité” asmi di yedhem Lounis Lounis ɣef tizlit-is " a lmus-iw” anda is yeqqar: "uffiɣ aɛrab di tefrka-w / serɣet-id s uḥalalas”. Meɛna tallit –nni tura tekfa. Ass-a bayger –nneɣ id nemestufa alarmi is yenna Zdek Mouloud:
Ay at ccna deg ilacacen
La ccenu azekka wi yeẓran
Anda-ken a wid yakk nessen
Anda –ken awid iɣ-icuban
Acimmi akka udrent wallen
Ay imdukal ay iḥbiben
Ay atmaten d imawlen
Ur sliɣ i nnan yeɛdawen
Ssliɣ-as i tsusmi-nwen
Tamla –iyi-d ayen din yellan”
Ait Slimane Hamid
Taneggarut n tneggura, d tagi n Saint Valentin i iḥerrem usalafist Hamadache. La d-yeqqar d leḥram, d lεada yessufuγen i ubrid, meḥsub mačči s adrar i tettawi.Γur-sen, tayri d leḥram. Ur ilaq ara ad tḥemmleḍ, neγ meqqar ḥemmel s tuffra. Ala lkerh i d-yeddan deg ucwari-nni-nsen. yenna-as Slimane Azem:’’bγiγ ad xedmeγ lemziyya, fkiγ-as claḍa i uγyul’’. Efk-as tura tajeğğit i taγadt, wali ma d asriḥi ara tt-tesriḥ neγ d lmakla ara tt-tečč? Ihi, ‘’azger yeεqel gma-s’’. Ussan-agi kan, Moussa Ismail i as-yennan ur ilaq ad heddren tamaziγt di lğameε. Yerna wagi d ccix zaεma. Meskin imi netta yessen kan yiwet n tmeslayt, iγil ula d Rebbi s taεrabt kan i yettmeslay. ‘’Muḥal ad fehmen, ur ssefhamen, d laẓ tilufḍa i d actil-nsen’’ i as-yenna Lwennas. Llan kra-nniḍen ufan-d akk ‘’lεilm anda yeffer’’. La ttεeddayen γer ttbaren, la asen-qqaren ur tennḍet ara crab daxel n lğernanat yuran s taεrabt axater yella wawal n Rebbi s daxel. Amek, ihi, ara as-yexdem win yeqqaren lğernan-agi n taεrabt? Yeqqim-d kan ad t-yesserγ. Lğernan n taεrabt srid γer tmes, γer ğahennama. Telha tagi! Neγ ma bγan ad qaddren leqran, ur t-id-ttarun ara deg yiγmisen. ‘’Wwin-d aγilif d yicwura n lkif, Hocine.M
Γer tmurt n lejdud gren-d asurif, Σebblen-d ad beddlen leεyud n udrar n nnif.’’ Ikemmel Lwennas deg wawal-is. Akken yebγu yili lḥal, Saint Valentin igerrzen i wid iḥemmlen. Xas yella yiwen n umeddakel yekreh Saint Valentin imi ass-nni swaswa i t-teğğa temeddakelt-is tuγal γer wayeḍ. Smaḥ, smaḥ kan ay ameddakel.
"Iḍelli-nni, tama n lagaṛ n Tizi-Wezzu ṭṭerḍqen sin ifaguten-nni ineggura n tmacint, d ifaguten n selɛa yedda-d yid-sen lɛeskar. Lagaṛ di lweqt-nni, d nettat i igan tamast: laman agemmaḍ-a di tama n temdint, tawaɣit agemmaḍ-in di tama nniḍen, ɣer wid izedɣen d lenda akkin, ger iḥedren d isennanen n ukeṛmus, tayerza n lḥif d llun-nni aberzegzaw n tferkiwin uzemmur. Di tmacint, imsukal akken ma llan tezdeɣ-iten tugdi. Tugdi-nni, Yeḥya yessen-itt ula d netta, ulamma mazal ur tt-yessin ara akken ilaq iwakken ad t-teḥerrem seg wayen ttwalint wallen-is”
Tukkist seg usebtar aneggaru
*Ungal n Nabil Farès ("Yahia Pas de Chance, un jeune homme de Kabylie”)
Yerra-t-id Ramdane Achab ar teqbaylit
Amer ad d-ḥkuɣ ɣef tin aɛzizen ad tt-wahmem. Dayen ur tettamnem. Asmi tt-waleɣ deg uɣerbaz qqleɣ d amedyaz. Mi d-zmumeg tefrari tagut, tcerq-d tafukt, tḥebbes tegrest, tefsa tefsut. Tesɛa allen d tiberkanin am iɛeqqayen n uzemmur, tawenza-s yeffer-itt wemzur-is, udem-is d amellal am udfel, tettfeǧǧiǧ am twizet. Ad as-tiniḍ d amekla yecban Isyaem i tt-ineǧren.
Seg wasmi tt-waleɣ, yerwel fell-i yiḍes, ḥettbeɣ itran deg yigenni. Ul-iw yal ass, yessaram ad tiwali i wakken as-yini acḥal aɛzizet fell-i, yerna ad as-d-ɣreɣ isefra isefra n tayri. Acḥal i tturǧiɣ deg urɣu n yiṭij, deg yicercuren n ugeffur, i ubeḥri yettcelwiḍen, deg udfel aqesḥan, i uqerrif n ugris d ubruri… Ɛeddan wussan rrnan iseggasen, iḍaq wul-iw yugi ad yesber. Xemmemeɣ ad as-ceggeɛeɣ tabret. Uriɣ-tt ulseɣ-as taɣuri acḥal n tikkal, seggmeɣ-tt akken iwata. Buxxeɣ-tt s leɛṭer, rniɣ-as tajeǧǧigt. Uzneɣ-as-tt, qqimeɣ ttraǧuɣ tirit. Ttraǧuɣ tḍul tmerǧa, ruḥ ay Aɛrab ar tafsut. Ul-iw yuyes tirit. Nniɣ-as i wul-iw, tikelt-a ma yella mmugreɣ-tt-id deg ubrid, ad ḍeggreɣ akin leḥya-agi ad as-iniɣ akk ayen tt-ḥulfuɣ, d wayen akk iqerḥen ul-iw, d wayen icebblen allen-iw. Yiwwas mmugreɣ-tt-id waḥd-s, ɛeddaɣ ad as-hedreɣ sqewqiweɣ, ɛerqen-iyi imeslayen. Ttergigiɣ, tafekka-w tekfel-itt-id tidi. Tɛedda-d zdat-i imi-w yelli maca awal ur t-id yuli. Mi dayen tɛedda, bdiɣ tt-lummuɣ deg yiman-iw:”Ayen a Bussaɛd i k-tenɣa leḥya, tɛedda-d waḥd-es, yerna abrid d ilem, ur as-tenniḍ acemma?”
Yiwwas mmugreɣ-tt-id waḥd-s. Walaɣ-tt t-tteddu-d deg ubrid-iw. Hegga-ɣ-d akk ayen i bɣiɣ ad as-tiniɣ. Hegga-ɣ-d ungal n tayri xedmeɣ-t am usefru. Mi d-wweḍ ar zdat-i, d ul-iw i as-yutlayen mačči d nekk-i:
-Nekkini d itri, zgiɣ ttidireɣ waḥd-i, asmi kem-walaɣ deg yigenni, ul-iw yeddegdeg, yerreẓ iruḥ d iceqfan. Steqseɣ wid-nni ijerben, inaẓuren, imusnawen, nnan-d akk ala kemm i izemren ad tt-dawiḍ ul ijerḥen.
-Nekk ur umineɣ s tmedyazt, d awalen kan, wa sdeffir wa, xas seggmen yerna cebḥen.
Temmuql-d s afus-iw, twala-d aqrab, tenna-d:
-Keččini d aselmad. Iselmaden ur sɛin ara azal ameqran di tmetti n wass-a acku ur ttaɣen ara aṭas n yidrimen. Nekk ad aɣeɣ ajenyur, amejjay neɣ bugaṭu.
-Nekkini d idrimen i bɣiɣ. D wigi i yessefraḥen. Ma d isefra akked d ijeǧǧigen, d timucuha kan, ḥku-tent-id kan di tmedyazt-ik. Boussad Ḥemar
Dɣa truḥ teǧǧa-id abeḥri.
Matoub: ‘’ma tγileḍ a Ğami ad kem-ayseγ…’’
Djamila: ’’muḥal ad t-ḥemmle&amp;gamma,; akken i ak-ḥemmleγ…’’<span style="white-space: pre;">
‘’Asmi ara d-yaweḍ lmijal,
Ddaw wakal ad d-nemqabal,
Mi ara neṭṭef abrid γer Rebbi…’’
Akka i as-d-yerra asmi ay tenwa lmut-is d asteεfu. Netta xas akken ur yemmut mi yemmut, yenna-as-d:
’’ Tγileḍ fniγ dayen thenna&amp;gamma,;
Di laxert steεfa&amp;gamma,;
Tγelṭeḍ di leḥsab-im…’’
Tizlit yecna deg useggas n 1993, d aciri γef wass-nni mi ara yemmet. Yeqqar-d amek i tt-yettrağu s ccuq melmi ara d-ternu γur-s i wakken ad mḥasaben dinna. Kra n lweqt mebεed tanṭel n Matub, truḥ Ğamila s aẓekka-s, tbedd din, la awal, la imeṭṭi, tettmektay-d tizlit-agi, ladγa anda i as-yeqqar:
’’Tγileḍ fniγ dayen thenna&amp;gamma,;
Nekk mazal uḍne&amp;gamma,;
D aṭṭan-im i d iyi-yewwin.
Si ṭṭhur, γer ṭṭhur zgiγ εusse&amp;gamma,;
Ameğğed ad as-sle&amp;gamma,;
S amḍiq-iw mi ara kem-id-εebbin.’’
Ahya a ddin uqabac a win iḥedren d acu ara as-yini neγ ahat d acu n tezlit ara as-d-iγenni mi ara mlilen. Meεna, iḥqa, wissen dγa ma ad mlilen, axater ‘’ulac anwa i d-yuγal, di lmut, i wakken ad aγ-d-yini…’’ Tadyant n Matub d Ğamila ulac-itt di tsekla n ddunit. Ula d Paulo Coello deg ungal-is ‘’Le Zahir’’ inuda-d akk amaḍal, kkes-d anda ur inuda γef tmeεcuqt-is meεna werğin yewweḍ γer laxert.
Tadyant n Matub d Ğamila tebda s ciṭ n dreε. Mi tt-id-yexḍeb, tella yakan, tettwaxḍeb. Meεna yenna-asen i yimawlan n Ğamila:’’tettwaxḍeb neγ ala, d nekk ara tt-yaγen.’’ Syin yuγ-itt. Acu aḥettem-a, tella sebba-s. uqbel ad yissin Ğamila, yessen yiwet n teqcict d tağaret-is. iḥemmel-itt, tḥemmel-it. Asmi yella di Fransa, tceyyeε γur-s teqcit-a u tenna-as ma s neyya-k ay telliḍ yid-i, ruḥ-d ad tt-nefru, neγ nekk yid-k berka, win i d-yusan ad zewğeγ. Ihi, Matub yefka-d tabrat i yiwen n’’umeddakel-is’’ anda i as-yenna ur ttεeṭṭileγ ara ad n-aseγ ad kem-id-xeḍbeγ. Winna, yeγra tabrat icerreg-itt. Iruḥ γer teqcict yenna-as d akken ur d-yettas ara u yenna-yi-d ur kem-yettaγ ara. Taqcict terkem seg urfan, winna yufa abrid γur-s. Zzin dayen kan, dγa yuγ-itt.
Ma d tamsalt n Ğamila, tebda s laεḍil: ass-nni n lexḍubegga-s, mi ttheggayent snat n twaculin, tawacult n Lwennas d tin n Ğamila, i lferḥ, Matub yesla s tmettant n Slimane Azem. Dγa, din din yeddem taqrabt-is, iruḥ γer Fransa. Lexḍubegga teqqim armi i d-yuγal. Am wakken neẓra Lwennas d win yettqadaren aṭas Slimane Azem. Yiwet n tikkelt yewwi-as akal n tmazirt n Slimane Azem i as-d-yeḍleb.
Amecwar-is d Ğamila yecna-t di tezlatin-is. Tudert-nsen ur telli d tuffirt. Di 7 n yiseggasen i sεaddan ‘’qlilit tmeqqwa n lehna…’’Akken armi d aseggas n 1988 mi t-yewwet uğadermi s ṛṣas, tkemmel tluγ liḥala gar-asen. Lwennas, yeẓra ur yezmir ara ad yesεu dderya. Seg wakken i tt-iḥemmel, yeḍleb-as ad t-teğğ ‘’Rwel skud teğğuğgeḍ, urez n lğedra yerka.’’. Γef tezlit-agi, dγa, i d-yella umqelleε gar-asen: nettat ur tebγi ara ad tt-id-yessufeγ. Tenna-as ma teffeγ-d d acu i d-yeggran gar-aneγ? Netta, yettwassen d aqerru n umcum, γer deffir ulac!
Xas d aqerru n umcum meεna d aḥeqqi, yesṭeεrif s tucḍiwin-is. Ayen akk i as-yexdem i Ğamila, yecna-t-id, yessenṭeq-tt-id di tezlatin. Gar-asent,
‘’Sebεa n lesnin i nesεedda,
Qqlilit tmeqqwa n lehna,
Ussan irkel d aγilif.
Deg uzal ur ak-ẓerreγ ara,
Deg yiḍ ur d-tkeccmeḍ ara,
Ay akken i ak-hedreγ kif kif.’’
Xas akken terwa-tent, meεna tḥemmel-it. Am wakken yemmut, tefka-as izen ad as-t-yawi i baba-s, tenna-as:
‘’Ma teẓriḍ baba, ini-as Ğamila,
leεteb-is yesfeḍ γer lqa (ε),
teffem-iyi s wid yemmuten.’’
Syin, Ğamila tezweğ akked…umeddakel-nniḍen n Lwennas. Truḥ d urgaz-is γer Kanada. Din, tesεa dderya. Ma d Lwennas yeqqim ugar n 3 n yiseggasen d uzgen netta d waṭṭan-is. D yiwen n umeddakel-is i t-irefden.
Iruḥ γer Kanada i wakken ad d-iẓer Ğamila. Yettγimi deg yiwet n lqahwa, yettrağu-tt din alamma tεedda-d i wakken ad tt-iwali. Mi d-yuγal, yuγ lḥal iruḥ γer Marikan. Nnan-as warraw n taddart-is: ‘’ansi akka i d-tekkiḍ a Lwennas? Yerra-asen-d: si ddunit ay At laxert!’’
Seg wasmi i t-teğğa Ğamila, Matub werğin yeḥbis ccna fell-as. Uzzu n tasa/tuzzma n temγart. Si ddaw uẓekka/ Imsefraγ/A lmeḥna.Tatut/Tannumi. Tameddit n wass/Tuzzma/ Tiγri n tağğalt. Qqurent tregwa/Ay iẓri-w yesriddimen. Ula album-is aneggaru, tella rriḥa n Ğamila.
‘’Mi as-nniγ ad kem-kerhe&amp;gamma,;
Ad kem-ḍummeγ seg wul-iw.
Dγa din i ttenṭarraye&amp;gamma,; Ssekraseγ lecγal-iw…’’ Hocine.M Mhenni Xalifi Bussaɛd Ḥemar
Tayri n Matub d Ğamila tuγal d amedya i medden. Mi yugi yiwen ad yettu tin iḥemmel, ad ak-d-yini ‘’Teḍra yid-i am Matub, ugiγ ad tt-ttuγ’’. Nacer-AKOUCHE
Dacu tettrajuḍ ay Amaziɣ? Cemten tutlayt-ik, huden taɣerma-k, srewten amezruy-ik.
Zrin 35 iseggasen ɣef tafsut n-imaziɣen id yellan deg useggas 1980. Tadyant id yegren i tikelt tamezwarut,s- lejher,tamsalt n-timmadit n Lẓẓayer ɣer unnar n-uskasi seg-imi tewwi tmurt tamunent –ines di 1962. Am akken zrin diɣen 14 n-iseggasen ɣef tafsut taberkant n 2001 id yeǧǧen ccwami-is deg ixfawen n-leqbayel wakali imi lejruḥ-is mazal ɣman. Imenɣi n-umussu n-leɛrac akked win n-warrac n-tafsut taberkent yesenquqel ( ahat i lebda?) tamuɣli n-imezdaɣ n-tmurt n-leqbayel ɣer tisertit imi ɣer wamur ameqqran deg-sen amennuɣ aserti s- wudem aqbur(akken i t uɣen imeɣnasen n-ssin ikabaren FFS d RCD d-umussu adelsan amaziɣ-MCB-) yeǧǧa-t lawan, ttwalint d-abrid ireglen ur nsufuɣ. Maca uqbel a nsuk tamuɣli ɣef taluft-agi, yelha lemmer ad nneg ṭelqa ara aɣ-yewwin si tazwara n-tamsalt alamma d taggara-s. Anect-a ad yilli s-lmendad n kra n-tuttriwin ara yillin d-timwelhin i uskasi nebɣa ad neger s-annar teɣzi n-waggur-agi n yibirir yellan d-amuli n-snat n- tegrawliwin-agi. Ɣef aya yelha ad nsuter seg tidmiwin-nneɣ aya-gi: Acu-tt ssebba n snat n-tafsutin-agi, yellan d yiwen umennuɣ xas ma mgaradent di ṣṣifa? Acu s-wacu id glant i yidles amaziɣ? Amek yella udem n-umennuɣ ɣef timadit tamaziɣt ass-a d-wamek ara yilli azekka?
Tamurt n-leqbayel deffir timunent:
Asmi yeffeɣ uṛumi deg useggas 1962, tamurt n-Leqbayel yufa-tt-id lḥal tezwi. Ur yelli id teǧǧa Franṣa seg-s. Amur ameqqran n-tuddar d-leḥwaṛi nhudent, ixxamen rraben, iberdan nexren, irgazen ya yemmut, wa iɛab, wa yenfa… ( hudden ḥerqen yixxamen, nɣan-aɣ izmawen, listiɛmar bu lemḥayen, yeǧǧa-d igujilen). Ifaden n-tmurt n-leqbayel merra tezwi-ten Fṛansa. Tadamsa( l’économie ) ulac, allalen n-tdawsa ( santé) d-asafar, iɣerbazen drus maḍi, iberdan xerben yerna xuṣṣen, Tizi-Wezzu s timad-is tella kan d-Lbilaj …kulci ixus. Ɣef lexṣaṣ-agi yenerna llaẓ akked lmiziriya imi imeḍqan n- lexdma, tafat, aman d-axayel kan i ten-ttxayalen imezdaɣ n-tmurt imiren. Di Lẓẓayer tamanaɣt aɣbel d-ayen nniḍen. D- amḥizwer ɣer ukersi n-leḥkem gar GPRA akked tarbaɛt yellan di Tunes. Amḥizwer yesyazeg tasilit n-lfetna. Widen yezdi umennuɣ ferqen myuɣalen d-icenga, s ddaw tiṭ i ttemyaxẓaren. Snat n-trabuyaɛ banent-d: tin n-Tlemcen ddaw tacdac-t n-Benbela, tin n-Tizi-Wezzu ddaw leɛnaya n Hocine Ait Ahmed. Maca lkil n-limizan imal ɣer terbaɛt n-Tlemcen acku iserdasen-is d wid id yekkan si tilist n Tunes (yellan ddaw leḥkem n Houari Boumedienne). Isardasen-agi ur ten-issum ara umenuɣ akked Franṣa, yerna ttuhaggen akken ilaq, begsen akken iwata ɣer yimenɣi. Ma yella d tarbaɛt n Tizi-Wezzu tsened ɣef yimjuhad id yesgra ṭrad akked Fṛansa. Tufa-ten-id tagnit aɛyen, ifaden kkawen. Rrnu ɣef anect-a tadyant n war amsefhem gar ssin imdebren n tmurt n leqbayel n yimiren Krim Belkacem akked Hocine Ait Ahmed imi temgared tmuɣli-nsen ɣef amek ara yilli umennuɣ mgal lbaṭṭel id teddun akken yesbur tacḍaḍt-is ɣef tmurt wakali. Ahat amennuɣ, ɣef akken id qqaren yimsenqaden n-unemzruy, ɣef tugdut d tilelli txesr-it tmurt n-leqbayel uqbel timunent s timad-is imi irgazen-is iṣaḥen, izemren ad qazmen taswiɛt, am Amirouche, Abane Remdane, Ali Mellah d-waṭas nniḍen, ɣlin d-imeɣrasen uqbel a tefru lgira. Deg aya tamurt n leqbayel tenzef irekeli. Tidyanin am " l’opération jumelle” ur d ǧǧin kra deg tanezmert tesɛa niqal( lawan n-trad akked urumi) tmurt n-leqbayel. D-anect-a d wayen nniḍen ( lexdaɛ, wer amsefhem gar imeɣnasen ) i-yeǧǧan tamurt n-leqbayel a tteknu i lweɛd, xas ulama teɛrreḍ amek ara terr aman ɣer tiregwa-nsen ddaw tacḍaḍt n-ukabar n-FFS deg useggas n 1963. Iswiyen yeḍfeṛ imiren ukabar n tirni n-iɣalen inemlayen d-aressi n-tugdut akked izerfan n- umdan d tilelli n-tidet di tmurt n Lẓẓayer wakali. Meɛna xas lebɣi yella, ifaden ulac. Amenuɣ ifuk s tweṭṭfa n- Mass Hocine Ait Ahmed ɣef lḥebs. Yemmut win yemuten di trad-nni, yettujeggeḥ win yettujegḥendi lwan deg daxal uderbuz n tsertit llant-d lemcawrat gar akabar FLN akked FFS ɣef wamek ara tefru tamselt-nni. Maca ur iɛaṭel-ara yezzi-d Boumedienne d-tarbaɛt-is ɣef uselway amenzu n tigduda n Lezzayer Benbela, iɣedel-it azekka-wen-nni n luffaq id yellan akked ukabar n FFS di 19 juin 1965. Yettkemil
Xas akken yerwel Hocine Ait Ahmed si lḥeb-s, akabar n FFS yekcem tudert tuffirt. Krim Belkacem yettwenɣa, Boudiaf Yenfa, iɣmisen wakali fkan annuz i udabu isedduyen timsal yecqan tmurt s-uzal akked tugdi ddaw leɛnaya n-wayen umi qqaren imiren asqamu agrawliw ( consiel de la revolution). Akabar n FLN yesenta tuccar-is tirni, armi ulac acu i-izemran ad yeḍṛu neɣ ad yennulfu mebla rrda n-ukabar-agi. Tamurt tesburr talaba n-tinemla tulmist( socialisme spécifique). D-anecta-agi yak id yufraren armi d-tagara n- isaggasen n 60. Maca di ttnaṣfa n-iseggasen n 70 bdant timsal tenfufuden-t. Tuɣalen waman ɣer lǧedra n-useklu n- umennuɣ ɣef izerfan d-wayen yeqnen ɣer-sen. S-tufra, s-lemḥadra s-ttawil n ccna akked isefra d-tisɣunin i teddun ddew uffus amenuɣ aserti yuɣal-d s-annar maca tikelt-a s-wudem nniḍen. lmeqṣud n-umenuɣ-agi d tigrin s-annar askasi mačči kan tikti n tugdut d-izerfan n-umdan imi ayen si ara d-yeglu aḥerkal n-isagassen n 70 d-tamselt n-nekwa n-tmurt yeqqimen tettuɛalaq seg asmi feclen igrawliyen iqbaylien n-umusu aɣelnaw ( mouvement national ) imesmaziɣen( berbérites) n-iseggasen n 1940/1950 am Benai Ouali, Mbarek Ait Menguellet, Ouamrane Idir, Laimeche Ali, Ali Yahya Rachid, Hocine Ait Ahmed,Amar Ould Hamouda….
Ait Slimane Hamid Syphax Y Syphax Y.
Mokrane Chikhi<span style="white-space: pre;">
Ilmend n tuffɣa n udlis «Abrid ɣer ukayad n Tmaziɣt" s tallelt n Tesbeddit Tiregwa, ara yili d aɛwin i warrac ara yesɛeddin ikayaden n BAK d BEM, nefren ad d-nessesten ameskar-is mass Lɛerbi Yeḥyun akken ad nesɛu ugar n yisallen fell-as. Hatan wayen iɣef nemmeslay.
Aɣmis n Yimaziɣen: Ahat Ad aɣ-d-tiniḍ tazwara anwa i d Lɛerbi i wid ur k-nessin?Mass Lɛerbi Yeḥyun, ilul deg Uqbu, aɣir n Bgayet. D aselmad n tutlayt d tsekla Tamaziɣt deg uɣerbaz alemmas n Yiɣil Ɛli. D yiwen umeɣnas i irefden amennuɣ ɣef tumast d yidles amaziɣ s wawal akked dira. Yura yakan ammud n yisefra i wumi isemma «Tayri n Umedyaz" i d-yeffɣen s lmendad n Usqamu Unnig n Timmuzɣa deg useggas n 2014.
Tessufɣeḍ-d taggara-a yiwen n udlis i yinelmaden ara yesɛeddin aBAK s tallelt n Tesbeddit Tiregwa, eg-aneɣ-d taḥawact fell-as…
Ad d-iniɣ kan, tanemmirt i kra n win d tin i d-yefkan afus n tallelt akken ad d-yeffeɣ udlis-iw u ad yaweḍ afus n unelmad, tanemmirt i kra n win i yi-d-yefkan tabɣest akken ad kemmleɣ tikli-w deg ubrid n tira, tanemmirt diɣen i kečč a M’henni ɣef tdiwennit-a. Ar tikkelt-nniḍen deg lehna.
n Murad Irnaten
"Di lǧerra-k ay awal…” d amud n tullisin n Murad Irnaten d-yefɣen ussan-a ɣer tezrigin Achab.
Atan cwiṭ deg wayen yuran deg usebtar aneggaru:
"Tira d tala yettaken aman I tara n ccfawat i waken ad tegmu. Aya d ayen n wala di tmettiyin ibeddent ɣef idelsan-nsent, tutlayin-nsent, d umezruy-nsent yettqadaren imyura-nsent, anida akken yal adlis yeḥrez amur si ccfawat, yal awal yeqqel i bab-is d ayla. Yal t ira d tirmit, d rreḍma n tudert i tutlayt. D tudert s unamek-ines ubriz, alqayan, ahrawan. Yal asekkil yella d aẓru amenzu i wawal yesrus umyaru ɣef lkaɣeḍ, yettfuki, yettnerni am waken yettfuki uɛeqqa n yirden di teɣzut yerẓa lmaɛun i tikkelt tamezwarut.
Yal tira tettak inzi ɣer tiɣwist-nni tamenzut swayes d-ikeččem umdan ɣer tudert. Yal awal d taẓunẓut, d aẓar i wejgagal n usenlfu”
Axxam n leqbayel d azamul n lbadna n tdukkli, d watas n t<span class="st">γ<em></em>awsiwin niden. Xas akken yemgarad di tmnadt <span class="st">γ<em></em>er tayed, ad t-tafed yesɛa yiwet n t<span class="st">γ<em></em>essa, yiwen n wazal. Qqaren-ak: «argaz d taftilt n berra, tamettut d taftilt n daxel" Acku lec<span class="st">γ<em></em>al n tmettut akk deg uxxam, d nettat i t-yesbeddayen, tetteg-as azal, fell-as i tesɛedday leɛmer-is akken ad ibedd wa ad iğğuğeg, axxam icudd <span class="st">γ<em></em>ef tmeṭṭut, ma yelha yewqa deg-s lxir d lbaraka, teḥsid d tameṭṭut nni i yelhan ma yewqa deg-s umennu<span class="st">γ<em></em> d yi<span class="st">γ<em></em>eblan yemme<span class="st">γ<em></em> di lḥif, neḥsid d tamettut ay dir, tesdehza deg uxxam-is.
Yal ta<span class="st">γ<em></em>awsa deg uxxam n leqbayen tesɛa anamek, seg unnu<span class="st">γ<em></em>en d teqbucin <span class="st">γ<em></em>er i<span class="st">γ<em></em>erban d sqef, <span class="st">γ<em></em>ef ayagi i ruḥe<span class="st">γ<em></em> <span class="st">γ<em></em>er tmurt akken ad issine<span class="st">γ<em></em> uger <span class="st">γ<em></em>ef uxxam aqbayli d wamek yemmug. Mi wwde<span class="st">γ<em></em>, tewwi-iyi setti <span class="st">γ<em></em>er uxxam aqdim, mi nekcem <span class="st">γ<em></em>er da<span class="st">γ<em></em>el n ubraḥ, tenna-iyi-d d akken irgazen zik, mi ara ad d-awden <span class="st">γ<em></em>er umdiq-agi, ilaq ad xedmen lḥess ara yeğğen tilawin n uxxam ad heggint iman-nsent, wa ssrent. Nkemmel akin deg ubrid wala<span class="st">γ<em></em> axxam yedrem, tenna-iyi-d setti akken wagi qqaren-as «axxam n Tmana", tteqsadent mi ara d-tekcem teslit axxam i tikkent tamezwarut ne<span class="st">γ<em></em> mi ara ad d-ilal uqcic, ayagi <span class="st">γ<em></em>ef lfal i yesɛa, syen tqubel-iyi-d yiwet n tewwurt s sin n lelwaḥ, tessebrareḥ-itt setti, nekk qqime<span class="st">γ<em></em> zdat n umnar, ma d nettat tebda la iyi-d-tettezzi amek yeddes uxxam-is, axxam anda tɛac.
Axxam n leqbayel yebda <span class="st">γ<em></em>ef sin yeḥricen: yiwen seg-sen d ameqqran, qqaren-as taqaɛet.ma d wayed mezzi fell-as qqaren-as adaynin.
Taqaɛet ne<span class="st">γ<em></em> agens ne<span class="st">γ<em></em> ti<span class="st">γ<em></em>er<span class="st">γ<em></em>ert d adeg anda ttqeggilen wat uxxam.ad tt-tafed teṭṭulem,imi ulac anda ara d-tekcem tafat anagar n yiwen n ṭṭaq amectuḥ anda i d-ikeccem ubeḥri. Ti<span class="st">γ<em></em>er<span class="st">γ<em></em>ert tettili texla madi.ur tettafed ṭṭabla wala taxzant wala akersiw, maca tella kan yiwet n t<span class="st">γ<em></em>awsa i yettilin di akk ixxamen: «azetta" wagi yezga-d akkin, <span class="st">γ<em></em>er u<span class="st">γ<em></em>reb i d-iqublen tawwurt. Win i wumi qqaren Tasga «mur de la lumière".ttarran azeṭṭa din imi anagar adeg-agi i d-tettawed mliḥ tafat n yiṭij, a<span class="st">γ<em></em>reb i d-iqublen Tasga qqaren-as «tinebdatin", wagi yezga-d rrif n tewwurt, Tinebdatin akked Tesga d inemgalen,imi Tinebdatin d azamul n tafat, <span class="st">γ<em></em>ef way-agi i ttcuddun lferḥ mi ara d-ilal uqcic <span class="st">γ<em></em>er Tesga, qqaren-ak «mi ara d-ilal uqcic ddesent tsegwa" ma d Tinebdatin «mur de l’obscurité" ttcuddun-t <span class="st">γ<em></em>er leḥzen am mi ara yemmet waldeɛad, qqaren-ak «mi ara yeffe<span class="st">γ<em></em> lmeyyet ttrunt tnebdatin"
Agens deg-s i ttilin lec<span class="st">γ<em></em>al n uxxam: lmakla d usewwi,ides d i<span class="st">γ<em></em>imi.ma tmuqled akin <span class="st">γ<em></em>er tqernit ak-id iban lkanun.ad tafed rsen s ufell-as yinyen deg-s sewwayen yerna sseḥmuyen di tegrest. S nnig lkanun yettili udekkan ttilint da<span class="st">γ<em></em>en tekwatin, rrif-s kan ad ak-id- iban use<span class="st">γ<em></em>wen, seg-s ttɛelliqen lebsel akk d ticcert. Ma tmuqled <span class="st">γ<em></em>er tama tazelmadt yella udaynin.deg-s yettili lmal d t<span class="st">γ<em></em>eṭṭen d tsita, imi wagi d azamul n rrbeḥ.maca adaynin ur yekmil ara srid i usgen tefreq iten yiwet n terkabt, deg udaynin yettili lmedwed deg-s i ttarran lqut i lmal-nni, s ufell-as tella t<span class="st">γ<em></em>imit. Syen tella teɛrict, deg-s ttağğan ikufiyen, wigi ttarran deg-sen rrezq.
S ddaw laɛnaya n useqamu unnig n timuzɣa, theyya-d t ɣiwant n At Wasif d comité des fḥtes n temdint n At Wasif rreḥba tamezwarut i tmedyazt n At Wasif (premières poésiades d At Ouacif). Tameɣra-agi ara i dumen tlala wussan d tajmilt i umedyaz n temnaṭ Lḥadj El Mokhtar Ait Said.Mebla tameɣra-agi i wumi iga irebbi Usqamu Unnig n Timuzɣa, ad d-tessekfel acḥal d amedyaz n temnaḍt n At Wasif.Ad d-nesmekti belli ussan-a n tmedyazt ad faken azekka n tlata Menas Abdelhak
Četkayen inelmaden n master 1 di tseddawit n akli muḥend ulḥaǧ di tubiret seg ugur iten-yemmugren aseggas-a d win icudden ɣer tnezduɣt n tseddawit(la citè universite) imi tuget n yinelmaden n uswir-a uffand iman nsen ur sɛin ara azref akken ad sԑun tixxamin di tnezduɣt n tseddawit, abeԑda inelmaden izedɣen berra lwilaya n tubiret am tizi uzzu, bumerdas, bgayet,msila dayen yeǧǧan inelamden-agi ar turra werԑad bdin leqraya alami id-uffan tifrat i uɣbel-a, ԑɛlaḥsab inelmaden wekden-d akken zedɣen di temnaḍin i yebeԑden azal n 30,40 yikilumiṭren ɣef tseddawit yerna ur zmiren ara ad as -ruḥun tisebḥiyin ad d-ttuɣalin tameddit ladɣa deg ussan n ccetwa am wid id-yezgan di tɣiwanin n seḥriǧ, at leqser, taqerbuzt, ṣur lɣuzlan, am wakken daɣen llan wid ara yeɣren ama d lxemsa n tmeddit ayaggi ur yettaf ara allalen n usiweḍ ɣer yixxamen nsen, ɣef wannect-a inelmaden ssuturen seg yimḍebren teԑna temsalt ad d-ggren iman nsen iwakken ad d-affen tifrat s lԑejlan akken ad bdun leqraya di tegnatin iwilmen mebla iɣublan. Mhenni Xalifi
Ahat ɣur ddeqs n medden, yemmug ugḍiḍ akken kan ad yidir tilelli-yis d afferfer deg yigenwan, ɣur wiyaḍ d lɛali-yas kan tiqeffet yettɣurrun akken ad n-yeǧǧ dinna tarwiḥt. Maca ɣur kra nniḍen, ur d agna-ya (choix) ur d wa i smenyifen, imi nutni ur ten-ttaǧǧan ttebrariɛen deg yigenwan, ur asen-meddin tiqefftin daɣen; wanag ttaɣen-ten-id s udrim sɣur yimrebbi-nsen seg ulzuz (ssuq) neɣ seg taddart, akken ad ten-id-ssekren ula d nutni deg uxxam, daɣen n tfergact (lqefs). Akken iban, mačči ɣef menwala n yigḍaḍ i la nettmeslay tura, zun ɣef uzeggaɛbur, abuḥeddad, neɣ d imdukkal-is. Maca, wid i d-ijebbden awellih n medden d wid yuqan, icebḥen, i yeɣlayen daɣen. Ɣef waya, imi babaɣayu ur yezmir yiwen ad t-iqerreb skud leḥsab n wazal-is s yimelyan, rnu wiss ma ad tafeḍ deg-s ayen akk tessarameḍ, rran ihi medden ɣer yigḍaḍ nniḍen i ten-yettcabin, ma neẓra belli qqersen-d seg yiwet n twacult, ed umi ssawalen tibiracin (tipirucin). Ɣas ur d-ttsaraxent ameslay n umdan am babaɣayuyat, maca deg ccna ẓewrent ayendin, deg ccbaḥa n tfekka-nsent daɣen skanayent-d ayen i asent-ihewwun i wallen n umecṭuḥ ed umeqqran. «Acḥal nekk d arebbi deg-sent almi uɣaleɣ nnumeɣ-itent, ur zmireɣ ad idireɣ ma ulac-itent". Ay d-yenna yiwen n yilemẓi yettrebbi-ten. Ma yella d ssuma n yibirucen-a, temgerrad seg yiwen ɣer wayeḍ, seg tewtemt ɣer uwtem, maca tettemtuttul gar 1500 n yidinaren almi d 2500 n yidinaren i uqerruy. Skud ur yewɛir usker-nsen, imi sran kan i waman akked tgella-nsen i yettnuzun, xilla n medden ttwalin deg-sen tadfi (plaisir) ugar n uqeddic. Menas Abdelhak
Taddart n lḥemmam i yetabaԑen ɣer tɣiwant n at raced id-yezgan deg usammer n lwilayt n tubiret d yiwet n taddart yettwasnen s wakal-is yelhan i tfellaḥt imi imezdaɣ n taddart-a xeddmen tafellaḥt,ɣas akka tettwasen s wannect-a yella wayen ixusen deg-s dayen iccuden ɣer lexsas n wallalen n tudert imi tettidir s waṭas iɣublan seg uɣbel ɣer wayeḍ, ɛlaḥsab iɣublan id-wekden imezdaɣ i uɣmis n yimaziɣen akken aɣbel ameqqran iten-icuɣben d tazeqqa n tujjya ( udawwi) imi ur sԑin ara anda ara d awwin imi tazeqqa yellan teɣlaq tiwwura-is azal n 10 yiseggasen-aya ar ass-a d wussan mazal-i-tt teɣlaq dayen yeǧǧan imezdaɣ n taddart-a ttafend iman nsen yesefk fell-asen ad ruḥen ɣer temnaḍin nniḍen iten- iqerben, imi ttruḥun ama d taɣiwant leqser iwakken ad sifsen liḥala ɣef umuḍin, si tama nniḍen wekden-d akken ayen yettnernin di leɛtab nsen lexsas n wallalen n usiwed dayen iweɛren ɣef twaculin ur yesɛin ara tikkeṛṛusin ilaq fell-asen kkeru n tkkeṛṛusin seg taddart nsen alami d sbiṭṭar n leqser s suma yettawḍen ɣer 500, 600 idinaren, ayaggi ur yeḥbis ara kan da imi aɣbel n lekwaɣeḍ yettkemmil ɣef yimezdaɣ iwakken ad d-yexdem yiwen lkaɣeḍ n leɛqed neɣ leԑmer neɣ ayen nniden ilaq ad iruḥ alami d taɣiwant n at raced, gar iɣublan nniḍen aman n tissit imi ttruḥen yal ass,lgaz n temdint, ur sɛin ara annar n waddal ideg ara yuraren yilmeẓyen rnu ɣur-s tazeqqa n yidles, lexsas n trisiti n yiberdan i yeǧǧan tugdi ad teɣli fell-asen ladɣa deg ussan n tegrest, ula d inelmaden si tama nsen sḥisfen ɣef lmeḥna ideg llan imi rwan ula d nutni leԑtab sebba n lexsas n wallalen d lebɛed n tkubaniyin anda qqaren ladɣa wid yeqqaren berra n taddart ama d wid yettruḥen ama d tasnawit n leqser neɣ tasnawit at raced, llan daɣen wid yeqqren deg uɣerbaz alemmas i yellan deg assif n lexmis imi beɛden s waṭas ɣef taddart ttefɣen seg yixxamen tafejrit ur d-ttuɣalen alami d lxemsa n tmeddit, ayaggi akk d iɣublan iten-yettmagaren d wuguren iten-yeṭṭafaren yal ass di tudert nsen,ɣef waya imezdaɣ n taddart nnan-d akken taddart nsen tettwaɛzel,ɣer taggra imezdaɣ ssaramen seg yimḍebren n tɣiwant akken ad rren lwelha nsen ɣef liḥala ideg ttidiren s yiṣenfaren unegmu i lfayda n yimezdaɣ i yettwaɣen si yal tama d tifrat s lɛejlan am wayen yeԑnan tazeqqa n tujjya,iwakken ad asen -sneqsen lmerta d lmeḥna iten-ixenqen.
Llan kra n yimdanen, nwan awi-d kan ad d-afen tifrat i wugur xas ulamma ad d-xelqen wayeḍ yugaren amezwaru-nni. Ɣur-sen, meɛlic d tayerza n ulɣum, ayen akk i d-yekrez ad t-yerkeḍ. D ṣṣaḥ, imdanen sḥassfen imi iberdan n tmurt ččuren d ammus, uɣalen d igudiyen mebla tilas. Aṭas i yettlummun wid-nni iḥebbsen s ṭunubilat ɣer tama n ubrid, tessen, syin ṭtaǧǧan tiqreɛtin dinna, ttembbabbayent ta ɣef ta alamma tewweḍ d taffa. Aya yettak udem n ddir i twennaṭ akked yimezdaɣ-is. Acu kan, ilaq ad iwali bnadem tidet s yiwet n tmuɣli, mačči s tneḥyaf neɣ s wuden n ddin kan. Ugur n wammus mačči d tamsalt n wid itessen kan, d tamsalt n yimezdaɣ akken ma llan. ‘’Wid itessen, ṭeggiren tiqreɛtin, wid yettẓallan, ṭeggiren iḍuman’’ i aɣ-d-yenna yiwen umezdaɣ. Llan kra, ɣillen ufan-asen-d tifrat i wugur-a. Kkren ssan akk leryaf n ubrid d tiqreɛtin n lbirra i wakken ur ḥebbsent ara tkeryas dinna. Ɛlaḥsab-nsen, ma ur ḥbisent ara ur d-yettili ara uḍegger n teqreɛtin. Acu kan, ttun yiwet n lḥaǧa: d nutni i yeččuren rrif n ubrid s teqreɛtin, ayen icemten nezzeh iberdan. Ula d wid yebɣan ad ḥebsen ma yettuḥettem fell-asen, ur d-ttafen ara amek, ur d-ttafen ara ciṭ n umekkan ilem. Daymi qqaren: ’’ad yekkat aɣyul, ad yettdari taberda’’. Yerna, tifrat, tella ɣer tudrin n tmurt n leqbayel. Tella ɣer taddart n Zoubga akked Yigersafen d tiyaḍ-nniḍen. D imedayaten limer yella ‘’cit n ṣswab maḍi, maḍi’’.
Et puis, akken i as-yenna winna: ‘’Ḥemmleɣ tayri d waman ṣemmneḍ,
Ḥemmleɣ ajeǧǧig n tefsut,
Ḥemmleɣ lemwansa n tmeṭṭut.
I merde i win iruḥen,
Ɣer lgirra yegla s tefruyt.
Awit-d un coup, awit-d sin,
Di lxater n wid yemḥemmalen,
Di lxater n wid yessefruyen.
I merde i wid iruḥen,
Ɣer lgirra akken ad nɣen,
Ɣer lgirra akken ad mten.’’ Hocine.M
<span style="white-space: pre;"> Hocine.M
Am waɣiren merra n tmurt, aṭas n tdukkliwin i d-yennulfan deg Bgayet deg yiseggasen ineggura; d ayen i mu nessawal amussu asduklan (mouvement associatif). Tal tidukkla amek tqeddec, tal yiwet deg wanwa aḥric i tefren ad d-tbin. Skanayent-d dɣa iqeddicen igerrzen, daha ed dihin, deg teɣzi n useggas, i ubaɣur n yimdanen s umata. Seg tdukkliwin-a aṭas i yellan, ɣas mačči kifkif i ttḥerrikent; imi llant ttxussunt deg wallalen, tiyaḍ deg tedrimt, tiyaḍ deg ufus, tiyaḍ nniḍen deg lebɣi idumen. Ma nemmeslay-d kan akka ɣef kra n tdukkliwin i d-ibanen xilla aseggas-a deg wannar-a n leqdic alsan (humanitaire), neɣ xersum i neẓra nekni, war ma nga leḥsab alqayan. Yettusemma neẓra ad ilint tidak i nettu. Ad d-nini kan tga ayen igerrzen Tdukkla n Ugezdu n Tujjya n Tesdawit n Bgayet s teɣlamt tasnujjyant i txeddem i tɣiwanin, akked tigawin nniḍen i txeddem i yimuḍan. Tidukkla i Yimeɛḍar ed Yimuḍan Idumen «Tiɣri", tga ula d nettat daɣen ddeqs n warmuden ar tura segmi d-tennulfa deg tlemmast n useggas-a. Iɛeggalen-is d wid ixedmen ccɣel yelhan ama deg tɣiwant n Ayt Smaɛel neɣ berra-yis. Tidukkla n Yimuḍan n Tgeltemt n Tezmalt tɛerreḍ daɣen ad d-terr yella wayen ur nelli, i lfayda n wid mu yekkes waṭṭan tikli. Am tirzi n tukksa ɣef lxaṭer i Uweqqas, i yettwassudsen deg unebdu yezrin. Tidukkliwin i iqeddcen ɣef yimuḍan n uqerruy, aṭas daɣen i yettazzalen da ed din, snulfuyent-asen-d kra n tegnatin n ucmummeḥ, am DEFI n Uweqqas, Tidukkla n yimuḍan n uqerruy n Bgayet, akked tin «Taɣect n Ugrud", ed tiyaḍ… Amḍan-a i d-nebder d kra seg-sent kan, wamma neẓra caḍent tdukkliwin i yettarran ddhen-nsent i wid ixussen ed wid yuḍnen. Ad yessirem kan umdan ad idum waya! Salima.D
D lewhayem! mazal ar ass-a timetti-nneɣ tettwali aṭṭan-agi n sida d ucenna neɣ d aṭabu ɣas ulamma aṭṭanen i merra tettmeslay fell-asen, ula d aṭṭan-nni n lkunsir tekkes-as awal-nni: ad aɣ-yenju rebbi yenju lmumnin! yettɣid win ara ihelken di tmurt-nneɣ,imi si tazwara iban kan ad yettuxeṭṭi ama sɣur medden ama sɣur-s, waya ad t-ncudd qbala ar nekkni ur nezri tidet n waṭṭan-a n abribus n VIH i yuɣalen ass-a seg waṭṭanen yezgan s dwawi d-snulfant tmura yeddan d wamek yettanṭaḍ imi nekkni ɣur-neɣ ma nemmeslay d win ihelken ad aɣ-yenṭeḍ,ma neḍsa-as ad aɣ-yenṭeḍ?dɣa ma nemsalam yid-s tenger fell-aɣ, Xaṭi!abirus n VIH yettanṭad s tuzzuft (sexualité ),s tsegnatin-nni yettwasnen deg uksum n win yuḍnen,ula ljerḥ amectuḥ yezmer ad as-yili d tawwurt i ubirus-a ma yemlal yid-s war ma nettu tyemmat t-issenṭaḍen i mmi-s ama di tadist neɣ s usuṭṭeḍ. Deg useggas n 2014 iban-d wazal n36,9 n yimelyan n wid ihelken sida maca mačči d leḥsab iseḥḥan imi aṭas n wid iteffren leḥlak-nsen, Dɣa ma nesteqsa acimi? tiririt tban kan imi s yes i d-nebda ameslay d acu kan imi nekkni nettwali ala s yir tiṭ, mi nesla s walbaɛd ihlek neqqar-as yekcem iberdan -nni n yir tuzzuft war ma nezra d acu n sebba s tidet imi yezmer ad tili d ayen nniḍen s wakka nettkemmil i taluft am wakken i as-yettkemmil win yuḍnen imi sida ur d-yettban ara s amdan arma f kant 7 ar 10 n yiseggasen d asawen bexlaf ccirat-nni timeẓyanin ur nettawi lewhi ɣur-s d ayen ara t-yeǧǧen ad yezzuzur deg ubirus -agi. D acu kan ayen yessewhamen imnadiyen d tamurt-a tageswaḥt tineslemt akk d tid i tt-icuban anda tuzzuft d leḥram ma teffeɣ i lɛada n zwaj meɛna mazal yettnerni sida deg-s! u acimi ur d-tettili ara tikci n yiḥaraben (préservatifs ) baṭel am wakken xeddment tmura irebḥen? i wakken ad nessenɣes talilit n waṭṭan-agi icudden deg ugar 80% n tikkwal ar tuzzuft.
Isem ‘’Azeffoun’’.Isem Azeffoun, yal wa uɣur i t-yeqqen. Llan kra qqaren-d awal Azeffoun, qqaren-t s tmeslayt tatergit i umekkan anda yettnejmaɛ waḍu. S tcelḥit, ad t-naf d taseǧǧigt neɣ d islem (La langouste). Ma d wiyaḍ, nnan-d yekka-d seg wawal ‘’Uzzaf’’, d tawrirt iɛezlen. Wwḍen armi i qqnen awal Azeffoun ɣer taɛrabt, nnan-d yekka-d seg ‘’Ɛaazifun’’, meḥsub wid yekkaten agambar. Ula d acennay El Ankis, d wa i d rraw-is. Ɣef wakken i aɣ-d-yenna Mass Amar Aridj, aselway n tiddukla ‘’Tigemmi’’. Imezwura ɣer taddart d Ifiniqeyyen, semman-as ‘’Ressirin’’. Syin d Ṛruman, semman-as ‘’Ruzuzus’’. Tettwabna deg 200 n yiseggasen uqbel talallit n¨ Ɛissa. Gar useggas n 248 d 251, yella yeḥkem-itt Decius. Ad t-naf deg ( Comptes kabyles n Camille Lacoste Dujardin)Ma d tamdint n tura yellan ɣer rrif n lebḥar i yewwin ula d nettat isem-agi ‘’Azeffoun’’, tebna-tt Fransa deg yiseggasen-nni 1870. Tsemma-as ‘’Port-Gueydon’’, d tajmilt i l’amiral Comte Louis Henri de Gueydon. Llant ttidirent deg-s 367 n twaculin n yirumyen, Iṭelyanen d Isbenyulen, 24 n twaculin n wudayen d 7 n twaculin n yiqbayliyen.
Lḥemmam n Ṛruman.Ar tura mazal kra n leḥyuḍ-is ttwabedden. Mazal tasebbalt-nni d tregwa ansi i d-ttruḥun waman ɣur-s. Nnan-d ttruḥun-d tlata n leṣnaf n waman: isemmaḍen, wid yemmuzeɣlen akked yiḥmayanen. Xedmen ttawil i wanect-a. Ṛruman, ḥemmlen asteɛfu akked lḥemmamat.
Imɣi ‘’Tajrumit’’ akked Ṛruman. S kra n wanda i yella yimɣi-agi n tejrumit, ḥṣuk-id ɛeddan syin Ṛruman. Acuɣer?Nnan-d d akken xeddmen yis-s aṭas n leṣnaf n tissit, ladɣa, Ricard. Nesteqsa ɣef wamek i t-xeddmen, ur d-nufi ara tiririt. Tessen-tt, diɣ, am latay d ddwa neɣ i uqraḥ n uɛrur.
Lǧameɛ lekbir.Lǧameɛ-agi, yebna-t winna yebnan lǧameɛ lekbir n Lezzayer tamanaɣt akked winna n Bgayet. Acu kan, taqubbet n wagi, tesqef s uqerrum. Ala netta i yellan deg tmurt n Lezzayer. Asmi i tella Fransa deg taddart-a, tesseqdec taqubet-a, d taɛessast imi tzemreḍ ad twaliḍ ɣer yal tama.
Ṣelṭan akked yelli-s.Nnan-d ṣelṭan n taddart-agi yesɛa kan yiwet n yelli-s. Ihi, i wakken ad tt-yefk, yecreḍ d akken argaz i yebɣan ad tt-yaɣ, ad yexdem ayen yessewhamen. Kkren sin mecqarwen gar-asen: yiwen yenna-as, ad ak-d-ssaliɣ aman seg lebḥar s tɣunam, wayeḍ yenna-as, ad ak-d-awiɣ aman seg Temgudt, azal n 50 n kilumitr. Kkren bdan lecɣal-nsen. Iɛedda lweqt, winna i d-yewwin aman seg Temgudt, yebda la d-yettqarrib. Ihi, yekker winna n tɣunam, isekker ahraḥu deg taddart am wakken dayen yessaweḍ-d aman. Mi yesla winna-nniḍen, dɣa, yeḥbes. Acu kan, yelli-s n ṣelṭan ur tt-yuɣ yiwen. Tenɣa iman-is. Wissen ayen?
Taqṣiṭ n umcic d ubehlul.Mi nerza ɣer tmeqqbert-nni n taddart, nufa azal n 25 n yiẓekwan n yiwet n twacult meḍlen deg yiwen umekkan, weḥd-sen. Nesteqsa, nnan-aɣ-d taqṣiṭ-a. Ur d-nettader ara isem n twacult. Tella yiwet n twacult, tedda d Fransa. Iɛeggalen-is, zgan tteḥqaren yiwen akken ubehlul. Anda i t-id-mmugren, ad ttmesxiren yis-s. Armi d yiwen wass, yerfed-d amcic, iḍegger-it s ufella n sqef n yiwen uxxam u yenna-as: ‘’ur d-tettṣubbuḍ ara syin alamma mmuten akken ma llan iɛeggalen n twacult-a.’’ Syin, ttmettaten yiwen, yiwen.
Kra n wudmawen.Mačči d yiwen neɣ d sin i yellan d anaẓur ameqqran n tama-agi. Nebɣa ad nẓer sser n waya. Yenna-d Mass Amar Aridj, yella ɣur-i, yerna mačči sser, ha-t-aya: ‘’ ihi, ad d-greɣ tiɣri i wid yebɣan ad uɣalen d inaẓuren imeqqranen, ad d-rzun ɣur-neɣ seg 24 duǧember i wakken ad sɛeddin yid-neɣ 40 n yussan n lyali. Agemmuḍ d yiswi, yettwaḍman. Deg lyali-a, llan 40 wussan, ferqen ɣef wussan, llant tcebḥanin n wass, llant tberkanin n yiḍ. Syin, 20 wussan-nniḍen, llant tberkanin n wass, tcebḥanin n yiḍ. Agu, ur tettwaliḍ ara sdat-k. Ad tefɣeḍ deg leɛqel-ik. Nuɣal akk d iderwicen. Acu kan, tidderwect n da, d taẓuri anda-nniḍen. Inaẓuren-agi akk imeqqranen, fɣen lawan n lyali-agi. Syin, s kra n win ara d-yuɣalen, leqrar-is deg Lwed Ɛisi.’’
<span style="white-space: pre;"> Hocine.M
Ɣer tama n rreḥba t-is snat n ssuq ( foire) n zzit n uzemmur id yellan deg Tizi-Wezzu zdat n teḥnayt n uxxam n tɣiwant aqbur si 15 ɣer 22 deg aggur n meɣres s ddemma n umezday n tfellaḥt n Tizi Wezzu, axxam n tannuzt n Tizi-Wezzu, axxam n tinzi( artisanat) n Tizi Wezzu akked usqamu n Lwilaya n Tizi- Wezzu, tella-d gar-nneɣ akked Mass Dahmane Cherif asefrak( gérant) n tkwebbanit taciṭa n tzemmurt ( branche d’olivier) yesɛan adeg( siège/site) deg At Jennad timlillit -agi deg id newwi awal ɣef lɣella n uzemmur akked iɣeblan icudden ɣer tanafrast( production) n zit n uzemmur deg tmurt n Leqbayel.
Amek i d-yufa iman-is Mass Dahmane Cherif deg uḥric-agi n taafrast n zzit n uzemmur?Tisin-iw ɣer uḥric-agi n tfellaḥt yesɛan azal meqqren ur d-yelli ara s ugacur imi aya werteɣ-t ɣef imawlan-iw yellan deg unnar-agi si zik n zik. Lejdud-iw xedmen deg uzemmur seg useggas 1830 ɣer ass-a n wussan. Zik s wudem aqbur (lemɛinṣrat tiqdimin) nekni tura nerna-d allalen atraren akked d tmuɣli tadamsant ɣer cɣel-agi. Nekni nella seg imezwura i d-skecmen timacinin timaynutin yeɛnan afres ( production ) n zzit n uzemmur, am akken d nekni id imezwura i inudan as-fkan udem atrar s tawil n timmumit-ines(mise en bouteille ) ddaw ticreṭ( marquee/ label).
Sani tessaweḍ tanafrast n zzit uzemmur taggara-agi?S umata yuɣal-d wazal i lɣella n zzit n uzemmur, a sbedd-i rreḥba yecban tagi ( tafeska n zzit n uzemmur) akked izumal n yemdanen id rezzun akken ad walin acu id nhegga d yiwen walɣuɣ id yessebganen amek terza taluft lɣaci. Tamsalt tella-asen deg ul. Akken simmal ad tt-nerni lqima n zzit uzemmur ilaq ad ddukklen iɣallen, acku zzit n uzemmur d yiwen uferdis di tdamsa i zemren ad yawi aṭas n reẓq i tmurt wakali…
Awal d kečč i t-id yenan s timmad-ik, tadamsa. Meɛna nekni nettwali d akken di tmurt-nneɣ ulac win srebḥent tizemrin-ines. Acu id ssebban waya?Ayen yeǧǧan, di tmurt n leqbayel, ur serbaḥent-ara tizemrin bab-nsen-t d imdebṛen( isekf ad nini imdegren) terza taluft n tfellaḥt, imi lqidaṛ deg ara ldin tiwwura i uɣellet n ṣṣenf agi n tfellaḥt s wudem atrar, nitni zgant d iɛakkir mgal a mteddu-ines deg ubrid n yimal. Nekni yellan deg annar mačči d yiwen ugur id nettmagar akken lɣella-nneɣ a tesɛu ticreṭ-ines( label) s w acu ara ttettwassen akked d taɣra-ines ( qualité) s wacu ara tettweɛqel. Ilaq a n ẓẓer belli lbenna n zzit ur teɛdil ara si tama ɣer tayeḍ. Amedya zzit n At jennad yesɛa ṛṛuḥ-is, win n At Ɛabbas daɣen… Ɣef aya iswi-nneɣ ad nessiweḍ ad tuɣal zzit deg tiqraɛtin s lqaleb-nsen-t, s ticret-nsen akken yal zzit yellan ad tufrar, a tt-ṭṭef amkan-is di ssuq aɣelnaw, yerna ( ayen ala?) a tt-namer zzit n tmura nniḍen di ssuq agraɣlan.
Si melmi i tebda takwabbanit- -nwen leqdic-agi? Nebda cɣel-agi n usiǧǧew n zzit s wudem atrar dge useggas n 1987. Nniqal negga ṛṛeḥba di temdint n Freha. Tura ɣer-nneɣ qrib 20 isaggsen deg abrid-agi. Lebɣi-nneɣ d amek ara s nner azal i lɣella-agi, ad teffeɣ seg udem-is aqbur neɣ amensay (traditionnel) akken as nelli abrid ɣer tannuzt tagraɣlant (commerce international). S w akka ara tenerni tafarest (production) n zzit yerna ad tawi lfayda i wid is yellan di lmendad( imawlan n tizemrin akked imawlan n lemɛinsrat d wid yettarran zzit ɣer tiqerɛunin).
Wissen dɣa ṛṛeḥba am tagi id yellan dag-i deg Tizi-Wezzu ma teskfa i wakken ad terr azal i lɣella n zzit n uzemmur…amek id abrid akken a naweḍ ɣer iswiyen-agi id bedreḍ.. Yella ssuq n daxel, win n tmurt.. timliliyin am t-igi ilaq ad ɛumen-t akken a nḥaz yal tama di tmurt. Akken medden ad ferzen gar leṣnaf n zzit yellan.Aya di tazwara. Sin akkin ilaq daɣen a nekcem rreḥbat tigraɣlalin akken leǧnas nniḍen ad isinen azemmur–nneɣ, zzit n tmurt-nneɣ. Nekni s tkwabanit-nneɣ nekcem yekka di leqdic-agi usefhem akked usbuceɛ. Nettikki deg acḥal n tfaskiwin yecqan zzit n uzemmur ama di Tunes, Fṛansa, Lmaruk…Meɛna a ttikki –agi yella kan s tawil-nneɣ, s tezmert n yiman-nneɣ, ulac asnnad sɣuṛ imdebran n tfellaḥt akken ad nufrar amek ilaq di rreḥbat-agi tigraɣlanin anda la "conccurence” teǧǧhed mačči d izli.. acu ara d yexdem yiwen weḥdes zdat n tkwabaniyin n ṭalyen neɣ n Fṛansa…? S tewzzel n wawal zzit-nneɣ tesɛa lbenna ines i tt-yessemxalfen ɣef tiyaḍ.. lemmer le CALPRF ad yefk afus n talelt nezmer u leqrar a n ssiǧǧew lɣella –agi ɣer beṛṛa n tmurt akken ad terfed tadamsa, yerna ad tt-serbeḥ imawlan n tizemrin …
Tineggura-agi nettwali aṭas n iffelaḥen id yezzin ɣer uzzu n tizemrin, maca ṭṭaqqa seg-sen qqaren d akken tizemrin-agi n uzzu ur t idiren-t- ara aṭas..acu id ssebba?Ayen ilaq a nẓer d akken tizemrin agi n uzzu d aneqqel. Mačči d tinaṣliyin. Mi ara d nekks neqla akken a sen iwɛed amkan ur d iteddu ara ixf n uẓar n tejra. Ixf n uẓar-agi uẓar d netta i yeqqazen s talqay deg akal akken ad ijab aman. ɣef aya ur yettiɣzif ara lɛamur-nsen-t. Lemmer id ak terbiḥ ay ul tili d tiẓebjin tinaṣliyin ara yettwaleqmen. Tidak sɛant aẓar d anaṣli, ttidiren d leqrun.
Amek ara s nneg udem amguran ( industriel) i senɛa agi n zzit uzemmur?Ilaq zzit ad tettejmaɛ ɣer yiwen umkan anda ara yuɣal ddaw yiwet n ticret( label). Sin akkin ilaq ad ɛummen imeḍqan n uzenzi i w akken ɛad ad yewweḍ ɣer tiḥuna timecṭaḥ neɣ tiḥuna timeqqranin ( grandes surfaces). Simmal ɛumment tikwabaniyin yesɛan label-nsen, simmal yettili-d u mzizzel, ɛaned gar-asent? d tismin-agi ara s yeggan azal i zzit ad acku amsaɣ ad yesɛu nnuba lextyar gra lmarka-agi akked d tihin. Ilaq zzit, am yal aferdis i keččmen ɣer ssuq, ad yekcem deg urar n "lbɛi u cra”. D ssuq ara iḥekmen mačči d-isemṣaren.
Ugur nniḍen tettmaggar tafellaḥt –agi n uzemmur tizemmrin ur ttarwent-ara yal aseggas…Aya icudd ɣef lxedma n w akal, afras n tizemrin. Nekni di tmurt n leqbayel nefres tizemrin lawan n ulqad.. xuḍi afras n tizemrin isefk ad yili deg aggur n Meɣres akkin d asawen…
Awal aneggaru i yimeɣṛiyen-nneɣ?Ilaq d lawan akken yal yiwen ad iẓer belli zzit n uzemmur ma yella yettwexdem s lmul, deg-s lfayda tameqqrant i bab-is, i tmurt( tadamsa n tmurt). Ass-a zzit n uzemmur d yiwen usafar yesɛayicen timura s lekmal ( am Surya, Tunes) ayen ɣer-nneɣ nekni ala? Ɣef aya ilaq as nner azal, ad naf iberdan amek zzit n tmurt-nneɣ a teɣzu leswaq ibeṛṛaniyen, ur telli-ara kan d lɣella n at wexxam..
Ait Slimane Hamid Abdelhak Menas
Twekded tneɣaft n ttrebga taɣenawt ahil n ikayaden uḥric wis kraḍ umbaɛd aqeɛed i texddem tneɣlaft ttrebga nuriya ben ɣebrit d akken ad bdun seg ayyur agi ideg i nella 15 si maggu deg yiswiren yemxalafen ama deg iɣbazen (amenzu,alemmas, tasnawit ), aqeɛed-agi i tesbed tneɣlaft ttrebga yussa-d umbaɛd aṭas n tmesbaniyin i xeddmen inelmaden n lwilayat unẓul n tmurt mi yella ayagi deg ayyur n remḍan yunyu, anda inelmaden-a ssuturen si ben ɣebrit awexer n yikayaden acku lwilayat n unẓul ttwasnent s lḥuman qessiḥen, dayen yeǧǧan taneɣlaft n ttrebga ad tbeddel rray terrat ɣer 15 mayyu meḥsub aswir 1,2, 3,4 deg uɣerbaz amenzu, ma yella d aswir 1, 2,3 deg uɣerbaz alemmas ma d 1,2 di tesnawit, Ma yella d ikayaden useldem ad bdun si 12 yunyu imi d tagnit ara farṣen yinelmaden. Ma yella d ikayaden n taggar yemxalafen am wayen ye3nan akayad n taggara deg uɣerbaz amenzu ad yili 22 may, akayad n taggara aswir wis 4 deg uɣerbaz alemmas ad yebdu si 24 ɣer 26 may, ma d akayad n taggara di tesnawit ad yebdu si 29 may ad ikemmel di 02 yunyu umbaɛd ad bdun imuras unebdu si 07 yulyu, am wakken ad tilli tuɣalin ɣer uɣerbaz aseggas ajdid deg ass n tlata 30 ɣuct i yixeddamen d wid ixeddmen di tedbelt, 01 september ttuɣalin lecyax d yiselmaden, ma yella d arrac ad uɣallen ass n lḥed 04 september, ihi abeddel -agi deg ahil n yikayaden yella-d ɣef tmesbaniyin warrac unẓul imi ur bɣin ara d-illin ikayaden di remḍan.
Deg zik-is, Tala-Xlil d yiwet n taddart iǧehden nezzeh deg lεarc n At Dwala di tmurt n Leqbayel.Taddart deg-s aṭas n yiderma d yirgazen n at yiɣil d wat ufud, rebεin n yirgazen s tmira, rebεin-niḍen war timira. Qqaren-d ḥekmen s ẓẓur ɣef tudrin i ten-id-iqerben, tekksen-asen ula d timecṛaḍ. Mi ara ruḥen ad d-kksen timecṛeḍt i webεaḍ n tudrin ttceyyiεen kan rebεin n yirgazen. Ma ruḥen rebεin n yirgazen s tmira, rebεin-nni war timira ad qqimen, ad qablen ma yella-d kra n cekk fell-asen, ad inin nekni ur nesεi ara di taddart annect-a n yirgarzen isεan timira. Ma d rebεin-nni war timira i iṛuḥen, rebεin-nni n yirgazen isɛan timira d nutni iqablen, ad inin am yimezwura. Yiwet n tikkelt, mmsawalen yimeqqranen n tudrin-nni ɣef i iεedda ẓẓuṛ ad nnejmaεen, ad mcawaṛen acu d wamek ara xedmen akken ad ḥerzen ɣef yiman-nsen d nnif-nsen. Yal taddart, tuzen-d tlata n yirgazen, lamin d sin n ṭemman ad mlilen di Tala n At Dwala. Wwḍen s amekkan, qqimen zzin d agraw ttmeslayen yiwen, yiwen; mi yekfa yiwen ad yuɣal wayeḍ. Iṣella-d yiwen ɣef sin yiberdan yenna: ‘‘ llah mselli aεlik ya ṛasul llah, llah mselli aεlik ya ṛasul llah’’ dɣa ibda awal. ‘’Ay atmaten, ayen iḍran yid-neɣ teẓramt, iḍra ula yid-wen. Kksen lmal i yimeksawen-nneɣ, kksen-aɣ timecṛeḍt, ittwakkes sser fell-aɣ. Tura ma nnejmeε ass-agi dagi di Tala n At Dwala alammi tewweḍ tkerza s aḥdid, alammi tewweḍ tfidi ɣer yiɣes,ifukk ṣbeṛ, issefk akken nella, akken i d-nnejmeε ass-agi, ad nedukkel ur nettɣimi ara nemferwazeε am ibawen ɣef lluḥ, yak teẓram awal nnan-t imezwra: bḍu-ten terniḍ-ten. Ihi ass-agi issefk fell-aɣ ad nedukkel, ad nemtawa-t ɣef yiwen n ṛṛay, ad nbedd ɣef yiwen wawal, ad nekfu-t cedda i d-iɣlin fell-aɣ, nekk deg wawal kfiɣ, ma sxesreɣ εfut-iyi, ma uqmeɣ ḥemdullah.’’ Wid i-as-id-izzin, nnan-d akk d awal n lεali. Rnan-d di lǧeṛṛa-s wiyaḍ, mtawan ɣef yiwen n ṛṛay ad d-suddsen yiwet n tmecṛeḍt ara isdukklen akk tudrin-nni akken ara d-sbedden daɣen yiwet n taggayt n yirgazen n at yiɣil ara iqamren wid ad d-iṛuḥen ad asen-kksen timecreḍt. Ssuq i-d-iḍefren anejmu&amp;epsilon,; sewqen imeqqranen n tudrin-nni, uɣen-d izgaren ara immezlen. Yal taddart txelleṣ ayen i as-d-tewwi n yidrimen a laḥsab n wazal n yimdanen i tesεa. Lexbeṛ n tmecreḍt iffeɣ, iwweḍ tudrin d leεruc, slan-as yis-s di yal tama n tmurt. Mmlalen yirgazen n tudrin-nni di Tala n At Dwala, ggan timecreḍt am tid yezrin, qedcen akken uɣen tanumi qedcen. Mmezlen yizgaren, igzem uksum, ibḍa d idura d tuna. Syin, sbeddent yiwet n taggayt n yirgazen n at ufud, wa yewwi abeckiḍ, wa d acaqur, wa d ajenwi, yal wa d acu n leslaḥ i iṭṭef ger yifassen-is. Ddurin isekla ttrajun wid ara d-yasen ad asen-kksen timecraḍt akken ad d-ẓedmen fell-asen, ad d-rren ttaṛ, ad tekfu cedda fell-asen. Wwḍen-d wid itekksen timecṛaḍ, isegras ɣef tuyat, ḥaren-d amzun d imnayen. Inṭeq-d yiwen seg-sen yenna i wid d-yufa ɣer tmecreḍt-nni: ‘’salamuεlikum ’’ Rran-as-id kra: ‘’salam ureḥmatellah lεeslama’’ Inṭeq-d wayed seg wid itekksen timecraḍ yenna: ‘’ah! Timecreḍt n tikkelt-a, tzad, tgerrez aksum-is llah ibarek d ayen kan!’’ Yerna-d wayeḍ di lǧeṛṛa-s yenna: ‘’d tidet! Aksum-a d aleqqaq ala i nekni iwumi ilaq!’’ Refden awal imeddukkal-is qqaren s utihi: ‘’aksum-a d aleqqaq ala i nekni iwumi ilaq! aksum-a d aleqqaq ala i nekni iwumi ilaq!’’ Adaoun Abdelghani
At yanni d yiwet temnaḍt n leqbayel i d-yezgan tama ɛlayen i ibeɛden s 40 km ɣef temdint n Tizi Uzzu. Tesɛan kraḍet n tɣiwanin gar-asent: At yanni, Ibudraren, d yiɛeṭṭafen. Ad naf tamnaḍt –agi tettwasen s waṭas n yinaẓuren n ccna am Ait Manguellat, Idir, Brahim izri d yimyura imeqqranen yecban Muloud Mammeri, neɣ wid yettwassnen s umezgun am Mohia, neɣ wid yeɣlin ɣef tmurt n Lezzayer, Amirouche Ait Hamouda. Ttwasnen Wat Yanni s tuṭṭfa deg leɛwayed d wansayen, gar-asen lxedma n uẓref ( lfeṭṭa). Lxedma–agi, dayen i d-ğğan lejdud–nsen. tTasuta tettak-itt i tayeḍ. Ad naf yal aseggas, lawan-agi, taggara n yulyu d tezwara n ɣuct, smektayen-d armud–agi ɛzizen fell-asen, aɛzizen ɣef leqbayel, s temsikeniyin ixeddmen deg taddart n Tewrirt Mimum deg tneɣriyin n uɣerbaz alemmas Lɛerbi At Aɛmer, deg uxxam n yilmeẓyen Keddache Ali akked yiwen umḍiq n yidles iwumi semman ( Espace culturel Mouloud Mammeri ). Imezdaɣ n temnaḍt-agi n Wat Yanni, qedcen akken iwata, abeɛda inelmaden n tesnawit Hsen Outaleb, imi win i d-yusan s tkerrust ad as-ttɛasen, ad as-mlen abrid i wid akk i d-yusan seg yal tama n Lezzayer s umata. Xedmen ahil seg wasmi tebda almi d asmi tekfa. Tebda ass n umhad 28 deg yulyu ɣef 10h 00, timsikent d lbiɛ n lfeṭṭa icebḥen dayen kan, tkemmel akken yal ass. Beddun ɣef 9h00 almi d 19hoo, Akka tekfa ass n 05 deg ɣuct s usenemmer n wid yettekin deg-s. Ad d-nernu ɣer waya aselway n tɣiwant n Wat Yanni Mass Smail deghoul d win yettaken afud i yal yiwen ixeddmen akken ad yenerni yidles n tmaziɣt. S lferḥ d ameqqran i d-yemeslay neɣ i d-yura ɣef teẓrigt-agi tis telṭac n tmeɣra n lfeṭṭa, rnu ɣur-s Mass Adal Arezki yettaken afus i yinelmaden yal mi ara yili usmekti n wayen akk icudden ɣer tmaziɣt. Tanemmirt-nsen, tanemmirt i yiḥeddaden n lfeṭṭa i as-yernan ccbaḥa i tmeṭṭut taqbaylit.
Zakia Ben yahia
S umata, tamsalmit n twermin tettban-d s tawla, anbeddal (talɣa d yinit) n twermin, d uqraḥ di lweqt n usebleɛ n yimetman.Tikkwal, llant kra n ccirat am uqraḥ n tɛdebbuḍt, tifidi deg uglim, ccirat n waṭṭan n turin d kra n yiwelsan di temgaṛt, yettefren neɣ i d-yettbegginen akken iwata lahlak-a.
